Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa

# Khuddakanikāye

## Vimānavatthupāḷi

### 1. Itthivimānaṃ

#### 1. Pīṭhavaggo

#### 1. Paṭhamapīṭhavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
<pb ed="T" n="0.0001" /> ‘‘Pīṭhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0001" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0001" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0001" /> te sovaṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkate malyadhare <note>mālyadhare (syā.)</note> suvatthe, obhāsasi vijjurivabbhakūṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="V" n="0.0002" /> taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena <note>moggalānena (ka.) evamuparipi</note> pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0002" /> puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0002" /> manussesu manussabhūtā, abbhāgatānāsanakaṃ adāsiṃ;
```

```
Abhivādayiṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ, yathānubhāvañca adāsi dānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamapīṭhavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Dutiyapīṭhavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0002" /> te veḷuriyamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkate malyadhare suvatthe, obhāsasi vijjurivabbhakūṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi <pb ed="T" n="0.0003" /> evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, abbhāgatānāsanakaṃ adāsiṃ;
```

```
Abhivādayiṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ, yathānubhāvañca adāsi dānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="0.0003" /> metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi <pb ed="V" n="0.0003" /> te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dutiyapīṭhavimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Tatiyapīṭhavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0003" /> te sovaṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkate malyadhare suvatthe, obhāsasi vijjurivabbhakūṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti <pb ed="T" n="0.0004" /> ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Appassa kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ <note>mametaṃ (ka.)</note>, yenamhi <note>tenamhi (ka.)</note> evaṃ jalitānubhāvā;
```

```
Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0004" /> virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
```

```
Tassa adāsahaṃ pīṭhaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Tatiyapīṭhavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Catutthapīṭhavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Pīṭhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0005" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0004" /> te veḷuriyamayaṃ uḷāraṃ, manojavaṃ gacchati yenakāmaṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkate malyadhare suvatthe, obhāsasi vijjurivabbhakūṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Kena <pb ed="V" n="0.0004" /> tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti <pb ed="T" n="0.0004" /> ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Appassa kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ, yenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā;
```

```
Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0005" /> virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
```

```
Tassa adāsahaṃ pīṭhaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi <pb ed="T" n="0.0006" /> te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Catutthapīṭhavimānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Kuñjaravimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Kuñjaro <pb ed="P" n="0.0005" /> te varāroho, nānāratanakappano;
```

```
Ruciro thāmavā javasampanno, ākāsamhi samīhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Padumi padma <note>paduma… (sī. syā.) evamuparipi</note> pattakkhi, padmuppalajutindharo;
```

```
Padmacuṇṇābhikiṇṇaṅgo, soṇṇapokkharamāladhā <note>… mālavā (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Padumānusaṭaṃ maggaṃ, padmapattavibhūsitaṃ.
```

```
Ṭhitaṃ vaggumanugghātī, mitaṃ gacchati vāraṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa pakkamamānassa, soṇṇakaṃsā ratissarā;
```

```
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, turiye pañcaṅgike yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa nāgassa khandhamhi, sucivatthā alaṅkatā;
```

```
Mahantaṃ accharāsaṅghaṃ, vaṇṇena atirocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Dānassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0005" /> te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
```

```
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchitā’’ti;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna <pb ed="T" n="0.0007" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0006" /> guṇasampannaṃ, jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ sataṃ;
```

```
Adāsiṃ pupphābhikiṇṇaṃ, āsanaṃ dussasanthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Upaḍḍhaṃ padmamālāhaṃ, āsanassa samantato;
```

```
Abbhokirissaṃ pattehi, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa kammakusalassa <note>kammassa kusalassa (sī. pī.)</note>, idaṃ me īdisaṃ phalaṃ;
```

```
Sakkāro garukāro ca, devānaṃ apacitā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ve sammāvimuttānaṃ, santānaṃ brahmacārinaṃ;
```

```
Pasanno āsanaṃ dajjā, evaṃ nande yathā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā hi attakāmena <note>atthakāmena (ka.)</note>, mahattamabhikaṅkhatā;
```

```
Āsanaṃ dātabbaṃ hoti, sarīrantimadhārina’’nti.
```

Kuñjaravimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Paṭhamanāvāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0006" /> nāvaṃ, nāri āruyha tiṭṭhasi;
```

```
Ogāhasi pokkharaṇiṃ, padmaṃ <note>padumaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> chindasi pāṇinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi <pb ed="T" n="0.0008" /> evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0007" /> manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
```

```
Disvāna bhikkhū tasite kilante, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0006" /> ve kilantāna pipāsitānaṃ, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti;
```

```
Sītodakā <note>sītodikā (sī.)</note> tassa bhavanti najjo, pahūtamalyā bahupuṇḍarīkā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ āpagā <note>tamāpagā (sī. ka.)</note> anupariyanti sabbadā, sītodakā vālukasanthatā nadī;
```

```
Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusasobhamānaṃ;
```

```
Tassīdha <note>tasseva (syā.)</note> kammassa ayaṃ vipāko, etādisaṃ puññakatā <note>katapuññā (sī.)</note> labhanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="0.0009" /> metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamanāvāvimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Dutiyanāvāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0007" /> nāvaṃ, nāri āruyha tiṭṭhasi;
```

```
Ogāhasi pokkharaṇiṃ, padmaṃ chindasi pāṇinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Kena <pb ed="M" n="0.0008" /> tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhutā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="T" n="0.0010" /> devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
```

```
Disvāna bhikkhuṃ tasitaṃ kilantaṃ, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ve kilantassa pipāsitassa, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti;
```

```
Sītodakā tassa bhavanti najjo, pahūtamalyā bahupuṇḍarīkā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ āpagā anupariyanti sabbadā, sītodakā vālukasanthatā nadī;
```

```
Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0007" /> bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusasobhamānaṃ;
```

```
Tassīdha kammassa ayaṃ vipāko, etādisaṃ puññakatā labhanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi <pb ed="T" n="0.0011" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0009" /> te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dutiyanāvāvimānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Tatiyanāvāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0008" /> nāvaṃ, nāri āruyha tiṭṭhasi;
```

```
Ogāhasi pokkharaṇiṃ, padmaṃ chindasi pāṇinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārā <pb ed="P" n="0.0009" /> nivesā te, vibhattā bhāgaso mitā;
```

```
Daddallamānā <note>daddaḷhamānā (ka.)</note> ābhanti, samantā caturo disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, sambuddheneva pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
```

```
Disvāna <pb ed="T" n="0.0012" /> bhikkhū tasite kilante, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ve kilantāna pipāsitānaṃ, uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti;
```

```
Sītodakā tassa bhavanti najjo, pahūtamalyā bahupuṇḍarīkā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0010" /> āpagā anupariyanti sabbadā, sītodakā vālukasanthatā nadī;
```

```
Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusasobhamānaṃ;
```

```
Tassīdha kammassa ayaṃ vipāko, etādisaṃ puññakatā labhanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārā <pb ed="V" n="0.0008" /> nivesā me, vibhattā bhāgaso mitā;
```

```
Daddallamānā ābhanti, samantā caturo disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te buddha mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsati;
```

```
Etassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0013" /> kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ, atthāya buddho udakaṃ apāyī’’ti <note>apāsīti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

Tatiyanāvāvimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Dīpavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="P" n="0.0010" /> vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tvaṃ vimalobhāsā, atirocasi devatā <note>devate (bahūsu) 83 vissajjanagāthāya saṃsandetabbaṃ</note>;
```

```
Kena te sabbagattehi, sabbā obhāsate disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0011" /> taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
```

```
Tamandhakāramhi timīsikāyaṃ, padīpakālamhi adāsi dīpaṃ <note>adaṃ padīpaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Yo andhakāramhi timīsikāyaṃ, padīpakālamhi <pb ed="T" n="0.0014" /> dadāti dīpaṃ;
```

```
Uppajjati jotirasaṃ vimānaṃ, pahūtamalyaṃ bahupuṇḍarīkaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Tenāhaṃ vimalobhāsā, atirocāmi devatā;
```

```
Tena me sabbagattehi, sabbā obhāsate disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi <pb ed="V" n="0.0009" /> te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dīpavimānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Tiladakkhiṇavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="P" n="0.0011" /> vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Kena <pb ed="M" n="0.0012" /> tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="T" n="0.0015" /> devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
```

```
Āsajja dānaṃ adāsiṃ, akāmā tiladakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyassa buddhassa, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Tiladakkhiṇavimānaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 11. Paṭhamapatibbatāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Koñcā <pb ed="P" n="0.0012" /> mayūrā diviyā ca haṃsā, vaggussarā kokilā sampatanti;
```

```
Pupphābhikiṇṇaṃ rammamidaṃ vimānaṃ, anekacittaṃ naranārisevitaṃ <note>naranārībhi sevitaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi <pb ed="M" n="0.0013" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0010" /> devi mahānubhāve, iddhī vikubbanti anekarūpā;
```

```
Imā <pb ed="T" n="0.0016" /> ca te accharāyo samantato, naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattāsi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, patibbatānaññamanā ahosiṃ;
```

```
Mātāva puttaṃ anurakkhamānā, kuddhāpihaṃ <note>kuddhāpahaṃ (sī.)</note> nappharusaṃ avocaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Sacce ṭhitā mosavajjaṃ pahāya, dāne ratā saṅgahitattabhāvā;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacittā, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi <pb ed="T" n="0.0017" /> evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamapatibbatāvimānaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

#### 12. Dutiyapatibbatāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Veḷuriyathambhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0014" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0013" /> ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ, vimānamāruyha anekacittaṃ;
```

```
Tatthacchasi devi mahānubhāve, uccāvacā iddhi vikubbamānā;
```

```
Imā ca te accharāyo samantato, naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattāsi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, upāsikā cakkhumato ahosiṃ;
```

```
Pāṇātipātā viratā ahosiṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Amajjapā no ca <note>nāpi (syā.)</note> musā abhāṇiṃ <note>abhāsiṃ (ka.)</note>, sakena <pb ed="T" n="0.0018" /> sāminā <note>sāmināva (sī.)</note> ahosiṃ tuṭṭhā;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacittā, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="0.0011" /> metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dutiyapatibbatāvimānaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

#### 13. Paṭhamasuṇisāvimānavatthu

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="M" n="0.0015" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0014" /> vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0019" /> manussesu manussabhūtā, suṇisā ahosiṃ sasurassa gehe <note>ghare (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
```

```
Tassa adāsahaṃ pūvaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Bhāgaḍḍhabhāgaṃ datvāna, modāmi nandane vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamasuṇisāvimānaṃ terasamaṃ.


```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

```
Sā <pb ed="P" n="0.0016" /> devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0020" /> manussesu manussabhūtā, suṇisā ahosiṃ sasurassa gehe.
```

#### 15. Uttarāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0017" /> taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="V" n="0.0013" /> devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Issā <pb ed="T" n="0.0021" /> ca maccheramatho <note>macchariyamatho ca (ka.)</note> paḷāso, nāhosi mayhaṃ gharamāvasantiyā;
```

```
Akkodhanā bhattuvasānuvattinī, uposathe niccahamappamattā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ, yā ca <note>yāva (sī. aṭṭha., ka. aṭṭha.) therīgāthāaṭṭhakathā passitabbā</note> pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā;
```

```
Saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca, vimānaṃ āvasāmahaṃ <note>āvasāmimaṃ (sī. aṭṭha., ka.) parato pana sabbatthapi ‘‘āvasāmahaṃ’’ icceva dissati</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viratā, musāvādā ca saññatā;
```

```
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārakā <note>āratā (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcasikkhāpade ratā, ariyasaccāna kovidā;
```

```
Upāsikā cakkhumato, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ sakena sīlena, yasasā ca yasassinī;
```

```
Anubhomi sakaṃ puññaṃ, sukhitā camhināmayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamahaṃ akāsiṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="0.0022" /> ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatīti.
```

§136. ‘‘Mama <pb ed="M" n="0.0018" /> ca, bhante, vacanena bhagavato pāde sirasā vandeyyāsi – ‘uttarā nāma, bhante, upāsikā bhagavato pāde sirasā vandatī’ti. Anacchariyaṃ kho panetaṃ, bhante, yaṃ maṃ bhagavā aññatarasmiṃ sāmaññaphale byākareyya <note>byākareyyāti (?)</note>, taṃ bhagavā sakadāgāmiphale byākāsī’’ti.

Uttarāvimānaṃ pannarasamaṃ.

#### 16. Sirimāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Yuttā <pb ed="P" n="0.0017" /> ca te paramaalaṅkatā hayā, adhomukhā aghasigamā balī javā;
```

```
Abhinimmitā pañcarathāsatā ca te, anventi taṃ sārathicoditā hayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘Sā tiṭṭhasi rathavare alaṅkatā, obhāsayaṃ jalamiva joti pāvako;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ varatanu <note>varacāru (katthaci)</note> anomadassane, kasmā nu kāyā anadhivaraṃ upāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmaggapattānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0014" /> yamāhunuttaraṃ <note>… nuttarā (ka.), anuttarā (syā.)</note>, nimmāya nimmāya ramanti devatā;
```

```
Tasmā kāyā accharā kāmavaṇṇinī, idhāgatā anadhivaraṃ namassituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure sucaritamācarīdha <note>sucaritaṃ acāridha (pī.)</note>,
```

```
Kenacchasi <pb ed="T" n="0.0023" /> tvaṃ amitayasā sukhedhitā;
```

```
Iddhī ca te anadhivarā vihaṅgamā,
```

```
Vaṇṇo ca te dasa disā virocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Devehi tvaṃ parivutā sakkatā casi,
```

```
Kuto cutā sugatigatāsi devate;
```

```
Kassa vā tvaṃ vacanakarānusāsaniṃ,
```

```
Ācikkha me tvaṃ yadi buddhasāvikā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Nagantare <pb ed="M" n="0.0019" /> nagaravare sumāpite, paricārikā rājavarassa sirimato;
```

```
Nacce gīte paramasusikkhitā ahuṃ, sirimāti maṃ rājagahe avediṃsu <note>avedisuṃ (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho ca me isinisabho vināyako, adesayī samudayadukkhaniccataṃ;
```

```
Asaṅkhataṃ dukkhanirodhasassataṃ, maggañcimaṃ akuṭilamañjasaṃ sivaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvānahaṃ amatapadaṃ asaṅkhataṃ, tathāgatassanadhivarassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Sīlesvahaṃ paramasusaṃvutā ahuṃ, dhamme ṭhitā naravarabuddhadesite <note>bhāsite (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Ñatvānahaṃ virajapadaṃ asaṅkhataṃ, tathāgatenanadhivarena <pb ed="T" n="0.0024" /> desitaṃ;
```

```
Tatthevahaṃ samathasamādhimāphusiṃ, sāyeva me paramaniyāmatā ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Laddhānahaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0018" /> amatavaraṃ visesanaṃ, ekaṃsikā abhisamaye visesiya;
```

```
Asaṃsayā bahujanapūjitā ahaṃ, khiḍḍāratiṃ <note>khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ (syā. pī.)</note> paccanubhomanappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ ahaṃ amatadasamhi <note>amatarasamhi (ka.)</note> devatā, tathāgatassanadhivarassa sāvikā;
```

```
Dhammaddasā paṭhamaphale patiṭṭhitā, sotāpannā na ca pana matthi duggati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Sā vandituṃ anadhivaraṃ upāgamiṃ, pāsādike kusalarate ca bhikkhavo;
```

```
Namassituṃ samaṇasamāgamaṃ sivaṃ, sagāravā sirimato dhammarājino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā <pb ed="M" n="0.0020" /> muniṃ muditamanamhi pīṇitā, tathāgataṃ naravaradammasārathiṃ;
```

```
Taṇhacchidaṃ kusalarataṃ vināyakaṃ, vandāmahaṃ paramahitānukampaka’’nti.
```

Sirimāvimānaṃ soḷasamaṃ.

#### 17. Kesakārīvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0025" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0015" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0019" /> vimānaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ, veḷuriyathambhaṃ satataṃ sunimmitaṃ;
```

```
Suvaṇṇarukkhehi samantamotthataṃ, ṭhānaṃ mamaṃ kammavipākasambhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Tatrūpapannā purimaccharā imā, sataṃ sahassāni sakena kammunā;
```

```
Tuvaṃsi ajjhupagatā yasassinī, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhasi pubbadevatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘Sasī adhiggayha yathā virocati, nakkhattarājāriva tārakāgaṇaṃ;
```

```
Tatheva tvaṃ accharāsaṅgaṇaṃ <note>accharāsaṅgamaṃ (sī.)</note> imaṃ, daddallamānā yasasā virocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Kuto nu āgamma anomadassane, upapannā tvaṃ bhavanaṃ mamaṃ idaṃ;
```

```
Brahmaṃva devā tidasā sahindakā, sabbe na tappāmase dassanena ta’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Yametaṃ sakka anupucchase mamaṃ, ‘kuto cutā tvaṃ idha āgatā’ti <note>kuto cutā idha āgatā tuvaṃ (syā.), kuto cutāya āgati tava (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Bārāṇasī nāma puratthi kāsinaṃ, tattha ahosiṃ pure kesakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhe <pb ed="T" n="0.0026" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0021" /> ca dhamme ca pasannamānasā, saṅghe ca ekantagatā asaṃsayā;
```

```
Akhaṇḍasikkhāpadā āgatapphalā, sambodhidhamme niyatā anāmayā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Tantyābhinandāmase svāgatañca <note>sāgatañca (sī.)</note> te, dhammena ca tvaṃ yasasā virocasi;
```

```
Buddhe ca dhamme ca pasannamānase, saṅghe ca ekantagate asaṃsaye;
```

```
Akhaṇḍasikkhāpade āgatapphale, sambodhidhamme niyate anāmaye’’ti.
```

Kesakārīvimānaṃ sattarasamaṃ.

Pīṭhavaggo paṭhamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Pañca pīṭhā tayo nāvā, dīpatiladakkhiṇā dve;
```

```
Pati dve suṇisā uttarā, sirimā kesakārikā;
```

```
Vaggo tena pavuccatīti.
```

#### 2. Cittalatāvaggo

#### 1. Dāsivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘Api <pb ed="V" n="0.0016" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0021" /> sakkova devindo, ramme cittalatāvane;
```

```
Samantā anupariyāsi, nārīgaṇapurakkhatā;
```

```
Obhāsentī <pb ed="T" n="0.0027" /> disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0022" /> taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, dāsī ahosiṃ parapessiyā <note>parapesiyā (ka.)</note> kule.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Upāsikā cakkhumato, gotamassa yasassino;
```

```
Tassā me nikkamo āsi, sāsane tassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmaṃ bhijjatuyaṃ kāyo, neva atthettha saṇṭhanaṃ <note>santhanaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sikkhāpadānaṃ pañcannaṃ, maggo sovatthiko sivo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Akaṇṭako agahano, uju sabbhi pavedito;
```

```
Nikkamassa phalaṃ passa, yathidaṃ pāpuṇitthikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘Āmantanikā raññomhi, sakkassa vasavattino;
```

```
Saṭṭhi <pb ed="P" n="0.0022" /> turiya <note>turiya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sahassāni, paṭibodhaṃ karonti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘Ālambo gaggaro <note>gaggamo (syā.), bhaggaro (ka.)</note> bhīmo <note>bhimmo (ka.)</note>, sādhuvādī ca saṃsayo;
```

```
Pokkharo <pb ed="T" n="0.0028" /> ca suphasso ca, viṇāmokkhā <note>vilāmokkhā (ka.)</note> ca nāriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Nandā ceva sunandā ca, soṇadinnā sucimhitā <note>sucimbhikā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Alambusā missakesī ca, puṇḍarīkāti dāruṇī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Eṇīphassā suphassā ca, subhaddā muduvādinī;
```

```
Etā caññā ca seyyāse, accharānaṃ pabodhikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Tā <pb ed="V" n="0.0017" /> maṃ kālenupāgantvā, abhibhāsanti devatā;
```

```
Handa naccāma gāyāma, handa taṃ ramayāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Nayidaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0023" /> akatapuññānaṃ, katapuññānamevidaṃ;
```

```
Asokaṃ nandanaṃ rammaṃ, tidasānaṃ mahāvanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ akatapuññānaṃ, idha natthi parattha ca;
```

```
Sukhañca katapuññānaṃ, idha ceva parattha ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṃ sahabyakāmānaṃ, kattabbaṃ kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Katapuññā hi modanti, sagge bhogasamaṅgino’’ti.
```

Dāsivimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Lakhumāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="P" n="0.0023" /> vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0029" /> puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Kevaṭṭadvārā nikkhamma, ahu mayhaṃ nivesanaṃ;
```

```
Tattha sañcaramānānaṃ, sāvakānaṃ mahesinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Odanaṃ kummāsaṃ <note>sākaṃ (sī.)</note> ḍākaṃ, loṇasovīrakañcahaṃ;
```

```
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtesu, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0024" /> upavasissaṃ, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā;
```

```
Saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca, vimānaṃ āvasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā <pb ed="V" n="0.0018" /> viratā, musāvādā ca saññatā;
```

```
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcasikkhāpade ratā, ariyasaccāna kovidā;
```

```
Upāsikā cakkhumato, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatīti.
```

‘‘Mama ca, bhante, vacanena bhagavato pāde sirasā vandeyyāsi – ‘lakhumā nāma,bhante,upāsikā bhagavato pāde sirasā vandatī’ti. Anacchariyaṃ kho panetaṃ, bhante, yaṃ maṃ bhagavā aññatarasmiṃ sāmaññaphale byākareyya <note>byākareyyāti (?)</note>. Taṃ bhagavā sakadāgāmiphale byākāsī’’ti.

Lakhumāvimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Ācāmadāyikāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍāya <pb ed="T" n="0.0030" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0024" /> te carantassa, tuṇhībhūtassa tiṭṭhato;
```

```
Daliddā kapaṇā nārī, parāgāraṃ apassitā <note>avassitā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Yā te adāsi ācāmaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Sā hitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, kaṃ nu sā disataṃ gatā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍāya me carantassa, tuṇhībhūtassa tiṭṭhato;
```

```
Daliddā kapaṇā nārī, parāgāraṃ apassitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Yā me adāsi ācāmaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Sā hitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, vippamuttā ito cutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Nimmānaratino nāma, santi devā mahiddhikā;
```

```
Tattha sā sukhitā nārī, modatācāmadāyikā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘Aho <pb ed="M" n="0.0025" /> dānaṃ varākiyā, kassape suppatiṭṭhitaṃ;
```

```
Parābhatena dānena, ijjhittha vata dakkhiṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘Yā mahesittaṃ kāreyya, cakkavattissa rājino;
```

```
Nārī sabbaṅgakalyāṇī, bhattu cānomadassikā;
```

```
Etassācāmadānassa<pb ed="T" n="0.0031" />, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘Sataṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0019" /> nikkhā sataṃ assā, sataṃ assatarīrathā;
```

```
Sataṃ kaññāsahassāni, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā;
```

```
Etassācāmadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘Sataṃ hemavatā nāgā, īsādantā urūḷhavā;
```

```
Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā, hemakappanavāsasā <note>hemakappanivāsasā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Etassācāmadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnamapi <pb ed="P" n="0.0025" /> dīpānaṃ, issaraṃ yodha kāraye;
```

```
Etassācāmadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasi’’nti.
```

Ācāmadāyikāvimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Caṇḍālivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Caṇḍāli vanda pādāni, gotamassa yasassino;
```

```
Tameva <note>taveva (sī.)</note> anukampāya, aṭṭhāsi isisattamo <note>isisuttamo (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘Abhippasādehi manaṃ, arahantamhi tādini <note>tādine (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Khippaṃ pañjalikā vanda, parittaṃ tava jīvita’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
Coditā bhāvitattena, sarīrantimadhārinā;
```

```
Caṇḍālī vandi pādāni, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
Tamenaṃ avadhī gāvī, caṇḍāliṃ pañjaliṃ ṭhitaṃ;
```

```
Namassamānaṃ sambuddhaṃ, andhakāre pabhaṅkaranti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇāsavaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0026" /> vigatarajaṃ anejaṃ, ekaṃ araññamhi raho nisinnaṃ;
```

```
Deviddhipattā upasaṅkamitvā, vandāmi taṃ vīra mahānubhāva’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇā jalitā mahāyasā, vimānamoruyha anekacittā;
```

```
Parivāritā accharāsaṅgaṇena <note>accharānaṃ gaṇena (sī.)</note>, kā tvaṃ subhe devate vandase mama’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0026" /> bhaddante caṇḍālī, tayā vīrena <note>therena (ka.)</note> pesitā;
```

```
Vandiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0032" /> arahato pāde, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ vanditvā <note>vanditva (sī.)</note> pādāni, cutā caṇḍālayoniyā;
```

```
Vimānaṃ sabbato bhaddaṃ, upapannamhi nandane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘Accharānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0020" /> satasahassaṃ, purakkhatvāna <note>purakkhitvā maṃ (syā. ka.)</note> tiṭṭhati;
```

```
Tāsāhaṃ pavarā seṭṭhā, vaṇṇena yasasāyunā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘Pahūtakatakalyāṇā, sampajānā paṭissatā <note>patissatā (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Muniṃ kāruṇikaṃ loke, taṃ bhante vanditumāgatā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
Idaṃ vatvāna caṇḍālī, kataññū katavedinī;
```

```
Vanditvā arahato pāde, tatthevantaradhāyathāti <note>tatthevantaradhāyatīti (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

Caṇḍālivimānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Bhadditthivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘Nīlā pītā ca kāḷā ca, mañjiṭṭhā <note>mañjeṭṭhā (sī.), mañjaṭṭhā (pī.)</note> atha lohitā;
```

```
Uccāvacānaṃ vaṇṇānaṃ, kiñjakkhaparivāritā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘Mandāravānaṃ pupphānaṃ, mālaṃ dhāresi muddhani;
```

```
Nayime aññesu kāyesu, rukkhā santi sumedhase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘Kena <pb ed="M" n="0.0027" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0027" /> kāyaṃ upapannā, tāvatiṃsaṃ yasassinī;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘Bhadditthikāti <note>bhadditthīti (sī.)</note> maṃ aññaṃsu, kimilāyaṃ upāsikā;
```

```
Saddhā sīlena sampannā, saṃvibhāgaratā sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘Acchādanañca bhattañca, senāsanaṃ padīpiyaṃ;
```

```
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtesu, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0033" /> pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā;
```

```
Saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca, vimānaṃ āvasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viratā, musāvādā ca saññatā;
```

```
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcasikkhāpade ratā, ariyasaccāna kovidā;
```

```
Upāsikā <pb ed="V" n="0.0021" /> cakkhumato, appamādavihārinī.
```

```
Katāvāsā katakusalā tato cutā <note>katāvakāsā katakusalā (ka.)</note>,
```

```
Sayaṃ pabhā anuvicarāmi nandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhū cāhaṃ paramahitānukampake, abhojayiṃ tapassiyugaṃ mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Katāvāsā katakusalā tato cutā <note>katāvakāsā katakusalā (ka.)</note>, sayaṃ pabhā anuvicarāmi nandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhaṅgikaṃ aparimitaṃ sukhāvahaṃ, uposathaṃ satatamupāvasiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Katāvāsā katakusalā tato cutā <note>katāvakāsā katakusalā (ka.)</note>, sayaṃ pabhā anuvicarāmi nandana’’nti.
```

Bhadditthivimānaṃ <note>bhadditthikāvimānaṃ (syā.)</note> pañcamaṃ.

```
Vaṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="0.0035" /> ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Soṇadinnāvimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Uposathāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="M" n="0.0029" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0029" /> vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…
```

```
Vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathāti maṃ aññaṃsu, sāketāyaṃ upāsikā;
```

```
Saddhā sīlena sampannā, saṃvibhāgaratā sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
‘‘Acchādanañca bhattañca, senāsanaṃ padīpiyaṃ;
```

```
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtesu, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā;
```

```
Saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca, vimānaṃ āvasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viratā, musāvādā ca saññatā;
```

```
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcasikkhāpade ratā, ariyasaccāna kovidā;
```

```
Upāsikā cakkhumato, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…
```

```
Vaṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="0.0036" /> ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkhaṇaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0023" /> nandanaṃ sutvā, chando me udapajjatha <note>upapajjatha (bahūsu)</note>;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ paṇidhāya, upapannamhi nandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘Nākāsiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0030" /> satthu vacanaṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Hīne cittaṃ paṇidhāya, sāmhi pacchānutāpinī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘Kīva ciraṃ vimānamhi, idha vacchasuposathe <note>vassasuposathe (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, yadi jānāsi āyuno’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhivassasahassāni <pb ed="M" n="0.0030" /> <note>saṭṭhi satasahassāni (?)</note>, tisso ca vassakoṭiyo;
```

```
Idha ṭhatvā mahāmuni, ito cutā gamissāmi;
```

```
Manussānaṃ sahabyata’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘Mā tvaṃ uposathe bhāyi, sambuddhenāsi byākatā;
```

```
Sotāpannā visesayi, pahīnā tava duggatī’’ti.
```

Uposathāvimānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 11. Dutiyabhikkhādāyikāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
```

```
Tassa adāsahaṃ bhikkhaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe. <pb ed="P" n="0.0034" />… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dutiyabhikkhādāyikāvimānaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

Cittalatāvaggo dutiyo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Dāsī <pb ed="M" n="0.0033" /> ceva lakhumā ca, atha ācāmadāyikā;
```

```
Caṇḍālī <pb ed="T" n="0.0040" /> bhadditthī ceva <note>bhadditthikā ca (syā.)</note>, soṇadinnā uposathā;
```

```
Niddā ceva suniddā ca <note>nandā ceva sunandā ca (sī.)</note>, dve ca bhikkhāya dāyikā;
```

```
Vaggo tena pavuccatīti.
```

Bhāṇavāraṃ paṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 3. Pāricchattakavaggo

#### 1. Uḷāravimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘Uḷāro <pb ed="V" n="0.0026" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0035" /> te yaso vaṇṇo, sabbā obhāsate disā;
```

```
Nāriyo naccanti gāyanti, devaputtā alaṅkatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘Modenti parivārenti, tava pūjāya devate;
```

```
Sovaṇṇāni vimānāni, tavimāni sudassane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘Tuvaṃsi issarā tesaṃ, sabbakāmasamiddhinī;
```

```
Abhijātā mahantāsi, devakāye pamodasi;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
```

```
Dussīlakule suṇisā ahosiṃ, assaddhesu kadariyesu ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhā sīlena sampannā, saṃvibhāgaratā sadā;
```

```
Piṇḍāya caramānassa, apūvaṃ te adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0036" /> sassuyācikkhiṃ, samaṇo āgato idha;
```

```
Tassa adāsahaṃ pūvaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Itissā <pb ed="T" n="0.0041" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0034" /> sassu paribhāsi, avinītāsi tvaṃ <note>avinītā tuvaṃ (sī.)</note> vadhu;
```

```
Na maṃ sampucchituṃ icchi, samaṇassa dadāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me sassu kupitā, pahāsi musalena maṃ;
```

```
Kūṭaṅgacchi avadhi maṃ, nāsakkhiṃ jīvituṃ ciraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘Sā ahaṃ kāyassa bhedā, vippamuttā tato cutā;
```

```
Devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ, upapannā sahabyataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Uḷāravimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Ucchudāyikāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘Obhāsayitvā <pb ed="V" n="0.0027" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0037" /> pathaviṃ <note>paṭhaviṃ (sī. syā.)</note> sadevakaṃ, atirocasi candimasūriyā viya;
```

```
Siriyā ca vaṇṇena yasena tejasā, brahmāva deve tidase sahindake <note>saindake (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ uppalamāladhārinī, āveḷinī kañcanasannibhattace;
```

```
Alaṅkate uttamavatthadhārinī, kā tvaṃ subhe devate vandase mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure kammamakāsi attanā, manussabhūtā purimāya jātiyā;
```

```
Dānaṃ suciṇṇaṃ atha sīlasaṃyamaṃ <note>saññamaṃ (sī.)</note>, kenūpapannā <pb ed="T" n="0.0042" /> sugatiṃ yasassinī;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
‘‘Idāni <pb ed="M" n="0.0035" /> bhante imameva gāmaṃ <note>gāme (syā. ka.)</note>, piṇḍāya amhākaṃ gharaṃ upāgami;
```

```
Tato te ucchussa adāsi khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacittā atulāya pītiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
‘‘Sassu ca pacchā anuyuñjate mamaṃ, kahaṃ <note>kahaṃ me (pī.)</note> nu ucchuṃ vadhuke avākiri <note>avākari (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Na chaḍḍitaṃ no pana khāditaṃ mayā, santassa bhikkhussa sayaṃ adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
‘‘Tuyhaṃnvidaṃ <note>tuyhaṃ nu idaṃ (syā.)</note> issariyaṃ atho mama, itissā sassu paribhāsate mamaṃ;
```

```
Pīṭhaṃ gahetvā pahāraṃ adāsi me, tato cutā kālakatāmhi devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
```

```
Devehi saddhiṃ paricārayāmahaṃ, modāmahaṃ kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
```

```
Devindaguttā <pb ed="T" n="0.0043" /> tidasehi rakkhitā, samappitā kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ puññaphalaṃ anappakaṃ, mahāvipākā mama ucchudakkhiṇā;
```

```
Devehi saddhiṃ paricārayāmahaṃ, modāmahaṃ kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0038" /> puññaphalaṃ anappakaṃ, mahājutikā mama ucchudakkhiṇā;
```

```
Devindaguttā tidasehi rakkhitā, sahassanettoriva nandane vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘Tuvañca <pb ed="M" n="0.0036" /> bhante anukampakaṃ viduṃ, upecca vandiṃ kusalañca pucchisaṃ;
```

```
Tato te ucchussa adāsi khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacitā atulāya pītiyā’’ti.
```

Ucchudāyikāvimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Pallaṅkavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘Pallaṅkaseṭṭhe <pb ed="V" n="0.0028" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0039" /> maṇisoṇṇacitte, pupphābhikiṇṇe sayane uḷāre;
```

```
Tatthacchasi devi mahānubhāve, uccāvacā iddhi vikubbamānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘Imā ca te accharāyo samantato, naccanti <pb ed="T" n="0.0044" /> gāyanti pamodayanti;
```

```
Deviddhipattāsi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, aḍḍhe kule suṇisā ahosiṃ;
```

```
Akkodhanā bhattuvasānuvattinī, uposathe appamattā ahosiṃ <note>appamattā uposathe (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Manussabhūtā daharā apāpikā <note>daharāsa’pāpikā (sī.)</note>, pasannacittā patimābhirādhayiṃ;
```

```
Divā ca ratto ca manāpacārinī, ahaṃ pure sīlavatī ahosiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā <pb ed="M" n="0.0037" /> viratā acorikā, saṃsuddhakāyā sucibrahmacārinī;
```

```
Amajjapā no ca musā abhāṇiṃ, sikkhāpadesu paripūrakārinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, pasannamānasā ahaṃ <note>atipasannamānasā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhaṅgupetaṃ anudhammacārinī, uposathaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0045" /> pītimanā upāvasiṃ;
```

```
Imañca ariyaṃ aṭṭhaṅgavarehupetaṃ, samādiyitvā kusalaṃ sukhudrayaṃ;
```

```
Patimhi kalyāṇī vasānuvattinī, ahosiṃ pubbe sugatassa sāvikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ kusalaṃ jīvaloke, kammaṃ karitvāna visesabhāginī;
```

```
Kāyassa bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ, deviddhipattā sugatimhi āgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
‘‘Vimānapāsādavare manorame, parivāritā accharāsaṅgaṇena;
```

```
Sayaṃpabhā devagaṇā ramenti maṃ, dīghāyukiṃ devavimānamāgata’’nti;
```

Pallaṅkavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Latāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
Latā <pb ed="P" n="0.0040" /> ca sajjā pavarā ca devatā, accimatī <note>accimukhī (sī.), acchimatī (pī. ka.) acchimutī (syā.)</note> rājavarassa sirīmato;
```

```
Sutā ca rañño vessavaṇassa dhītā, rājīmatī dhammaguṇehi sobhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
Pañcettha <pb ed="V" n="0.0029" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0038" /> nāriyo āgamaṃsu nhāyituṃ, sītodakaṃ uppaliniṃ sivaṃ nadiṃ;
```

```
Tā <pb ed="T" n="0.0046" /> tattha nhāyitvā rametvā devatā, naccitvā gāyitvā sutā lataṃ bravi <note>bruvī (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ uppalamāladhārini, āveḷini kañcanasannibhattace;
```

```
Timiratambakkhi nabheva sobhane, dīghāyukī kena kato yaso tava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘Kenāsi bhadde patino piyatarā, visiṭṭhakalyāṇitarassu rūpato;
```

```
Padakkhiṇā naccagītavādite, ācikkha no tvaṃ naranāripucchitā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, uḷārabhoge kule suṇisā ahosiṃ;
```

```
Akkodhanā bhattuvasānuvattinī, uposathe appamattā ahosiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘Manussabhūtā <pb ed="P" n="0.0041" /> daharā apāpikā <note>daharāsa’pāpikā (sī.)</note>, pasannacittā patimābhirādhayiṃ;
```

```
Sadevaraṃ sassasuraṃ sadāsakaṃ, abhirādhayiṃ tamhi kato yaso mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ tena kusalena kammunā, catubbhi ṭhānehi visesamajjhagā;
```

```
Āyuñca <pb ed="T" n="0.0047" /> vaṇṇañca sukhaṃ balañca, khiḍḍāratiṃ paccanubhomanappakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
‘‘Sutaṃ nu taṃ bhāsati yaṃ ayaṃ latā, yaṃ no apucchimha akittayī no;
```

```
Patino kiramhākaṃ visiṭṭha nārīnaṃ, gatī ca tāsaṃ pavarā ca devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘Patīsu <pb ed="M" n="0.0039" /> dhammaṃ pacarāma sabbā, patibbatā yattha bhavanti itthiyo;
```

```
Patīsu dhammaṃ pacaritva <note>pacaritvāna (ka.)</note> sabbā, lacchāmase bhāsati yaṃ ayaṃ latā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘Sīho yathā pabbatasānugocaro, mahindharaṃ pabbatamāvasitvā;
```

```
Pasayha hantvā itare catuppade, khudde mige khādati maṃsabhojano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva saddhā idha ariyasāvikā, bhattāraṃ nissāya patiṃ anubbatā;
```

```
Kodhaṃ vadhitvā abhibhuyya maccharaṃ, saggamhi sā modati dhammacārinī’’ti.
```

Latāvimānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Guttilavimānaṃ

1. Vatthuttamadāyikāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Sattatantiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0042" /> sumadhuraṃ, rāmaṇeyyaṃ avācayiṃ;
```

```
So <pb ed="T" n="0.0048" /> maṃ raṅgamhi avheti, ‘saraṇaṃ me hohi kosiyā’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0030" /> te saraṇaṃ homi, ahamācariyapūjako;
```

```
Na taṃ jayissati sisso, sissamācariya jessasī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0040" /> taṃ devi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā, moggallānena pucchitā;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘Vatthuttamadāyikā nārī, pavarā hoti naresu nārīsu;
```

```
Evaṃ piyarūpadāyikā manāpaṃ, dibbaṃ sā labhate upecca ṭhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā <pb ed="P" n="0.0043" /> me passa vimānaṃ, accharā kāmavaṇṇinīhamasmi;
```

```
Accharāsahassassāhaṃ, pavarā <note>accharāsahassassāhaṃ pavarā, (syā.)</note> passa <pb ed="T" n="0.0049" /> puññānaṃ vipākaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūtā yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

(Anantaraṃ caturavimānaṃ yathā vatthudāyikāvimānaṃ tathā vitthāretabbaṃ <note>( ) natthi sī. potthake</note>)
