31. Morahatthadāyikāvimānavatthu (20)

<p rend="hangnum">§573.</p>

```
Morahatthaṃ ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa…pe….
```

32. Chattadāyikāvimānavatthu (21)

<p rend="hangnum">§581.</p>

```
Chattaṃ <note>chattañca (ka.)</note> ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa…pe….
```

33. Upāhanadāyikāvimānavatthu (22)

<p rend="hangnum">§586.</p>

```
Upāhanaṃ ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa…pe….
```

34. Pūvadāyikāvimānavatthu (23)

<p rend="hangnum">§597.</p>

```
Pūvaṃ ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa…pe….
```

35. Modakadāyikāvimānavatthu (24)

<p rend="hangnum">§605.</p>

```
Modakaṃ ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa…pe….
```

36. Sakkhalikadāyikāvimānavatthu (25)

<p rend="hangnum">§613.</p>

```
‘‘Sakkhalikaṃ <note>sakkhaliṃ (sī. syā.)</note> ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa…pe….
```

<p rend="hangnum">§614.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā me passa vimānaṃ, accharā kāmavaṇṇinīhamasmi;
```

```
Accharāsahassassāhaṃ, pavarā passa puññānaṃ vipākaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§615.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="0.0037" /> metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§617.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me ajja, suppabhātaṃ suhuṭṭhitaṃ <note>suvuṭṭhitaṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Yaṃ addasāmi <note>addasaṃ (sī. syā.), addasāsiṃ (pī.)</note> devatāyo, accharā kāmavaṇṇiniyo <note>kāmavaṇṇiyo (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§618.</p>

```
‘‘Imāsāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0048" /> <note>tāsāhaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> dhammaṃ sutvā <note>sutvāna (syā. ka.)</note>, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ.
```

```
Dānena samacariyāya, saññamena damena ca;
```

```
Svāhaṃ tattha gamissāmi <note>tattheva gacchāmi (ka.)</note>, yattha gantvā na socare’’ti.
```

Guttilavimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Daddallavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§619.</p>

```
‘‘Daddallamānā <pb ed="T" n="0.0059" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0048" /> <note>daddaḷhamānā (ka.)</note> vaṇṇena, yasasā ca yasassinī;
```

```
Sabbe deve tāvatiṃse, vaṇṇena atirocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§620.</p>

```
‘‘Dassanaṃ nābhijānāmi, idaṃ paṭhamadassanaṃ;
```

```
Kasmā kāyā nu āgamma, nāmena bhāsase mama’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§621.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ bhadde subhaddāsiṃ, pubbe mānusake bhave;
```

```
Sahabhariyā ca te āsiṃ, bhaginī ca kaniṭṭhikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§622.</p>

```
‘‘Sā ahaṃ kāyassa bhedā, vippamuttā tato cutā;
```

```
Nimmānaratīnaṃ devānaṃ, upapannā sahabyata’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§623.</p>

```
‘‘Pahūtakatakalyāṇā, te deve yanti pāṇino;
```

```
Yesaṃ tvaṃ kittayissasi, subhadde jātimattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§624.</p>

```
‘‘Atha <note>kathaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena, kena vā anusāsitā;
```

```
Kīdiseneva dānena, subbatena yasassinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§625.</p>

```
‘‘Yasaṃ etādisaṃ pattā, visesaṃ vipulamajjhagā;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§626.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭheva piṇḍapātāni, yaṃ dānaṃ adadaṃ pure;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyassa saṅghassa, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§627.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§629.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0049" /> tayā bahutare bhikkhū, saññate brahmacārayo <note>brahmacarino (syā.), brahmacāriye (pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tappesiṃ annapānena, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§630.</p>

```
‘‘Tayā <pb ed="T" n="0.0060" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0038" /> bahutaraṃ datvā, hīnakāyūpagā ahaṃ <note>ahuṃ (ka. sī.)</note>;
```

```
Kathaṃ tvaṃ appataraṃ datvā, visesaṃ vipulamajjhagā;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§631.</p>

```
‘‘Manobhāvanīyo <pb ed="P" n="0.0049" /> bhikkhu, sandiṭṭho me pure ahu;
```

```
Tāhaṃ bhattena <note>bhadde (ka.)</note> nimantesiṃ, revataṃ attanaṭṭhamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§632.</p>

```
‘‘So me atthapurekkhāro, anukampāya revato;
```

```
Saṅghe dehīti maṃvoca, tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ kariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§633.</p>

```
‘‘Sā dakkhiṇā saṅghagatā, appameyye patiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Puggalesu tayā dinnaṃ, na taṃ tava mahapphala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§634.</p>

```
‘‘Idānevāhaṃ jānāmi, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ;
```

```
Sāhaṃ gantvā manussattaṃ, vadaññū vītamaccharā;
```

```
Saṅghe dānāni dassāmi <note>saṅghe dānaṃ dassāmihaṃ (syā.)</note>, appamattā punappuna’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§635.</p>

```
‘‘Kā esā devatā bhadde, tayā mantayate saha;
```

```
Sabbe deve tāvatiṃse, vaṇṇena atirocatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§636.</p>

```
‘‘Manussabhūtā devinda, pubbe mānusake bhave;
```

```
Sahabhariyā ca me āsi, bhaginī ca kaniṭṭhikā;
```

```
Saṅghe dānāni datvāna, katapuññā virocatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§637.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammena pubbe bhaginī, tayā bhadde virocati;
```

```
Yaṃ saṅghamhi appameyye, patiṭṭhāpesi dakkhiṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§638.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchito hi mayā buddho, gijjhakūṭamhi pabbate;
```

```
Vipākaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0061" /> saṃvibhāgassa, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§639.</p>

```
‘‘Yajamānānaṃ manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§640.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0050" /> me buddho viyākāsi, jānaṃ kammaphalaṃ sakaṃ;
```

```
Vipākaṃ saṃvibhāgassa, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§641.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 750; kathā. 798</note> ‘‘Cattāro ca paṭipannā, cattāro ca phale ṭhitā;
```

```
Esa saṅgho ujubhūto, paññāsīlasamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§642.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 751; kathā. 798</note> ‘‘Yajamānānaṃ manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§643.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 752; kathā. 798</note> ‘‘Eso <pb ed="V" n="0.0039" /> hi saṅgho vipulo mahaggato, esappameyyo udadhīva sāgaro;
```

```
Ete hi seṭṭhā naravīrasāvakā, pabhaṅkarā dhammamudīrayanti <note>dhammakathaṃ udīrayanti (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§644.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 753; kathā. 798</note> ‘‘Tesaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0050" /> sudinnaṃ suhutaṃ suyiṭṭhaṃ, ye saṅghamuddissa dadanti dānaṃ;
```

```
Sā dakkhiṇā saṅghagatā patiṭṭhitā, mahapphalā lokavidūna <note>lokavidūhi (syā. ka.)</note> vaṇṇitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§645.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 754; kathā. 798</note> ‘‘Etādisaṃ yaññamanussarantā <note>puññamanussarantā (syā. ka.)</note>, ye vedajātā vicaranti loke;
```

```
Vineyya maccheramalaṃ samūlaṃ, aninditā <pb ed="T" n="0.0062" /> saggamupenti ṭhāna’’nti.
```

Daddallavimānaṃ <note>daddaḷhavimānaṃ (ka.)</note> chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Pesavatīvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§646.</p>

```
‘‘Phalikarajatahemajālachannaṃ<pb ed="P" n="0.0051" />, vividhacitratalamaddasaṃ surammaṃ;
```

```
Byamhaṃ sunimmitaṃ toraṇūpapannaṃ, rucakupakiṇṇamidaṃ subhaṃ vimānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§647.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāti <pb ed="M" n="0.0051" /> ca dasa disā nabheva suriyo, sarade tamonudo sahassaraṃsī;
```

```
Tathā tapatimidaṃ tava vimānaṃ, jalamiva dhūmasikho nise nabhagge.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§648.</p>

```
‘‘Musatīva nayanaṃ sateratāva <note>sateritāva (syā. ka.)</note>, ākāse ṭhapitamidaṃ manuññaṃ;
```

```
Vīṇāmurajasammatāḷaghuṭṭhaṃ, iddhaṃ indapuraṃ yathā tavedaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§649.</p>

```
‘‘Padumakumuduppalakuvalayaṃ, yodhika <note>yūdhika (sī.)</note> bandhukanojakā <note>yothikā bhaṇḍikā nojakā (syā.)</note> ca santi;
```

```
Sālakusumitapupphitā asokā, vividhadumaggasugandhasevitamidaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§650.</p>

```
‘‘Saḷalalabujabhujaka <note>sujaka (sī. syā.)</note> saṃyuttā <note>saññatā (sī.)</note>, kusakasuphullitalatāvalambinīhi<pb ed="T" n="0.0063" />;
```

```
Maṇijālasadisā yasassinī, rammā pokkharaṇī upaṭṭhitā te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§651.</p>

```
‘‘Udakaruhā ca yetthi pupphajātā, thalajā ye ca santi rukkhajātā;
```

```
Mānusakāmānussakā ca dibbā, sabbe tuyhaṃ nivesanamhi jātā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§652.</p>

```
‘‘Kissa saṃyamadamassayaṃ vipāko, kenāsi kammaphalenidhūpapannā;
```

```
Yathā ca te adhigatamidaṃ vimānaṃ, tadanupadaṃ avacāsiḷārapamhe’’ti <note>pakhumeti (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§653.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="M" n="0.0052" /> ca me adhigatamidaṃ vimānaṃ, koñcamayūracakora <note>caṅkora (ka.)</note> saṅghacaritaṃ;
```

```
Dibya <note>dibba (sī. pī.)</note> pilavahaṃsarājaciṇṇaṃ, dijakāraṇḍavakokilābhinaditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§654.</p>

```
‘‘Nānāsantānakapuppharukkhavividhā, pāṭalijambuasokarukkhavantaṃ;
```

```
Yathā ca me adhigatamidaṃ vimānaṃ, taṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0064" /> te pavedayāmi <note>pavadissāmi (sī.), pavedissāmi (pī.)</note> suṇohi bhante.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§655.</p>

```
‘‘Magadhavarapuratthimena<pb ed="P" n="0.0052" />, nāḷakagāmo nāma atthi bhante;
```

```
Tattha ahosiṃ pure suṇisā, pesavatīti <note>sesavatīti (sī. syā.)</note> tattha jāniṃsu mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§656.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhamapacitatthadhammakusalaṃ<pb ed="V" n="0.0040" />, devamanussapūjitaṃ mahantaṃ;
```

```
Upatissaṃ nibbutamappameyyaṃ, muditamanā kusumehi abbhukiriṃ <note>abbhokiriṃ (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§657.</p>

```
‘‘Paramagatigatañca pūjayitvā, antimadehadharaṃ isiṃ uḷāraṃ;
```

```
Pahāya mānusakaṃ samussayaṃ, tidasagatā idha māvasāmi ṭhāna’’nti.
```

Pesavatīvimānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Mallikāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§658.</p>

```
‘‘Pītavatthe <pb ed="P" n="0.0053" /> pītadhaje, pītālaṅkārabhūsite;
```

```
Pītantarāhi vaggūhi, apiḷandhāva sobhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§659.</p>

```
‘‘Kā <pb ed="M" n="0.0053" /> kambukāyūradhare <note>kakambukāyuradhare (syā.)</note>, kañcanāveḷabhūsite;
```

```
Hemajālakasañchanne <note>pacchanne (sī.)</note>, nānāratanamālinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§660.</p>

```
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayā lohitaṅgamayā <note>lohitaṅkamayā (sī. syā.)</note> ca, muttāmayā <pb ed="T" n="0.0065" /> veḷuriyamayā ca;
```

```
Masāragallā sahalohitaṅgā <note>sahalohitaṅkā (sī.), sahalohitakā (syā.)</note>, pārevatakkhīhi maṇīhi cittatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§661.</p>

```
‘‘Koci koci ettha mayūrasussaro, haṃsassa rañño karavīkasussaro;
```

```
Tesaṃ saro suyyati vaggurūpo, pañcaṅgikaṃ tūriyamivappavāditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§662.</p>

```
‘‘Ratho ca te subho vaggu <note>vaggū (syā.)</note>, nānāratanacittito <note>nānāratanacittaṅgo (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Nānāvaṇṇāhi dhātūhi, suvibhattova sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§663.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmiṃ rathe kañcanabimbavaṇṇe, yā tvaṃ <note>yattha (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note> ṭhitā bhāsasi maṃ padesaṃ;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§664.</p>

```
‘‘Sovaṇṇajālaṃ maṇisoṇṇacittitaṃ <note>vicittaṃ (ka.), cittaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, muttācitaṃ hemajālena channaṃ <note>sañchannaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Parinibbute gotame appameyye, pasannacittā ahamābhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§665.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ kammaṃ karitvāna, kusalaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ;
```

```
Apetasokā sukhitā, sampamodāmanāmayā’’ti.
```

Mallikāvimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Visālakkhivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§666.</p>

```
‘‘Kā <pb ed="T" n="0.0066" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0054" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0054" /> nāma tvaṃ visālakkhi <note>visālakkhī (syā.)</note>, ramme cittalatāvane;
```

```
Samantā anupariyāsi, nārīgaṇapurakkhatā <note>purakkhitā (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§667.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="V" n="0.0041" /> devā tāvatiṃsā, pavisanti imaṃ vanaṃ;
```

```
Sayoggā sarathā sabbe, citrā honti idhāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§668.</p>

```
‘‘Tuyhañca idha pattāya, uyyāne vicarantiyā;
```

```
Kāye na dissatī cittaṃ, kena rūpaṃ tavedisaṃ;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§669.</p>

```
‘‘Yena kammena devinda, rūpaṃ mayhaṃ gatī ca me;
```

```
Iddhi ca ānubhāvo ca, taṃ suṇohi purindada.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§670.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ rājagahe ramme, sunandā nāmupāsikā;
```

```
Saddhā sīlena sampannā, saṃvibhāgaratā sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§671.</p>

```
‘‘Acchādanañca bhattañca, senāsanaṃ padīpiyaṃ;
```

```
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtesu, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§672.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ <note>catuddasiṃ (pī. ka.)</note> pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§673.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā;
```

```
Saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca, vimānaṃ āvasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§674.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viratā, musāvādā ca saññatā;
```

```
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§675.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcasikkhāpade ratā, ariyasaccāna kovidā;
```

```
Upāsikā cakkhumato, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§676.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā <pb ed="T" n="0.0067" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0055" /> me ñātikulā dāsī <note>ñātikulaṃ āsī (syā. ka.)</note>, sadā mālābhihārati;
```

```
Tāhaṃ bhagavato thūpe, sabbamevābhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§677.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathe cahaṃ gantvā, mālāgandhavilepanaṃ;
```

```
Thūpasmiṃ abhiropesiṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§678.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="0.0055" /> kammena devinda, rūpaṃ mayhaṃ gatī ca me;
```

```
Iddhī ca ānubhāvo ca, yaṃ mālaṃ abhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§679.</p>

```
‘‘Yañca sīlavatī āsiṃ, na taṃ tāva vipaccati;
```

```
Āsā ca pana me devinda, sakadāgāminī siya’’nti.
```

Visālakkhivimānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Pāricchattakavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§680.</p>

```
‘‘Pāricchattake <pb ed="V" n="0.0042" /> koviḷāre, ramaṇīye manorame;
```

```
Dibbamālaṃ ganthamānā, gāyantī sampamodasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§681.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
```

```
Dibbā saddā niccharanti, savanīyā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§682.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
```

```
Dibbā gandhā pavāyanti, sucigandhā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§683.</p>

```
‘‘Vivattamānā kāyena, yā veṇīsu piḷandhanā.
```

```
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, tūriye pañcaṅgike yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§684.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṭaṃsakā vātadhutā <note>vātadhūtā (sī. syā.)</note>, vātena sampakampitā;
```

```
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, tūriye pañcaṅgike yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§685.</p>

```
‘‘Yāpi <pb ed="P" n="0.0056" /> te sirasmiṃ mālā, sucigandhā manoramā;
```

```
Vāti <pb ed="T" n="0.0068" /> gandho disā sabbā, rukkho mañjūsako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§686.</p>

```
‘‘Ghāyase taṃ sucigandhaṃ <note>suciṃ gandhaṃ (sī.)</note>, rūpaṃ passasi amānusaṃ <note>mānusaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§687.</p>

```
‘‘Pabhassaraṃ accimantaṃ, vaṇṇagandhena saṃyutaṃ;
```

```
Asokapupphamālāhaṃ, buddhassa upanāmayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§688.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ kammaṃ karitvāna, kusalaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ;
```

```
Apetasokā sukhitā, sampamodāmanāmayā’’ti.
```

Pāricchattakavimānaṃ dasamaṃ.

Pāricchattakavaggo tatiyo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0056" /> –

```
Uḷāro ucchu pallaṅko, latā ca guttilena ca;
```

```
Daddallapesamallikā, visālakkhi pāricchattako;
```

```
Vaggo tena pavuccatīti.
```

#### 4. Mañjiṭṭhakavaggo

#### 1. Mañjiṭṭhakavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§689.</p>

```
‘‘Mañjiṭṭhake <pb ed="V" n="0.0043" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0057" /> <note>mañjeṭṭhake (sī.)</note> vimānasmiṃ, soṇṇavālukasanthate <note>sovaṇṇavālukasanthate (syā. pī.), sovaṇṇavālikasanthate (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Pañcaṅgike turiyena <note>turiyena (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, ramasi suppavādite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§690.</p>

```
‘‘Tamhā vimānā oruyha, nimmitā ratanāmayā;
```

```
Ogāhasi <pb ed="T" n="0.0069" /> sālavanaṃ, pupphitaṃ sabbakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§691.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa yasseva sālassa, mūle tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
So so muñcati pupphāni, onamitvā dumuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§692.</p>

```
‘‘Vāteritaṃ sālavanaṃ, ādhutaṃ <note>ādhūtaṃ (sī.)</note> dijasevitaṃ;
```

```
Vāti gandho disā sabbā, rukkho mañjūsako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§693.</p>

```
‘‘Ghāyase taṃ sucigandhaṃ, rūpaṃ passasi amānusaṃ;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§694.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, dāsī ayirakule <note>ayyirakule (syā. ka.)</note> ahuṃ;
```

```
Buddhaṃ nisinnaṃ disvāna, sālapupphehi okiriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§695.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṭaṃsakañca sukataṃ, sālapupphamayaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Buddhassa upanāmesiṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§696.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0057" /> kammaṃ karitvāna, kusalaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ;
```

```
Apetasokā sukhitā, sampamodāmanāmayā’’ti.
```

Mañjiṭṭhakavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Pabhassaravimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§697.</p>

```
‘‘Pabhassaravaravaṇṇanibhe<pb ed="P" n="0.0058" />, surattavatthavasane <note>vatthanivāsane (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Mahiddhike candanaruciragatte, kā tvaṃ subhe devate vandase mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§698.</p>

```
‘‘Pallaṅko <pb ed="V" n="0.0044" /> ca te mahaggho, nānāratanacittito <pb ed="T" n="0.0070" /> ruciro;
```

```
Yattha tvaṃ nisinnā virocasi, devarājāriva nandane vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§699.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure sucaritamācarī bhadde, kissa kammassa vipākaṃ;
```

```
Anubhosi devalokasmiṃ, devate pucchitācikkha;
```

```
Kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§700.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍāya te carantassa, mālaṃ phāṇitañca adadaṃ bhante;
```

```
Tassa kammassidaṃ vipākaṃ, anubhomi devalokasmiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§701.</p>

```
‘‘Hoti ca me anutāpo, aparaddhaṃ <note>aparādhaṃ (syā.)</note> dukkhitañca <note>dukkaṭañca (sī.)</note> me bhante;
```

```
Sāhaṃ dhammaṃ nāssosiṃ, sudesitaṃ dhammarājena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§702.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ taṃ vadāmi bhaddante, ‘yassa me anukampiyo koci;
```

```
Dhammesu taṃ samādapetha’, sudesitaṃ dhammarājena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§703.</p>

```
‘‘Yesaṃ atthi saddhā buddhe, dhamme <pb ed="T" n="0.0071" /> ca saṅgharatane;
```

```
Te maṃ ativirocanti, āyunā yasasā siriyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§704.</p>

```
‘‘Patāpena vaṇṇena uttaritarā,
```

```
Aññe mahiddhikatarā mayā devā’’ti;
```

Pabhassaravimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Nāgavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§705.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṅkatā <pb ed="M" n="0.0058" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0059" /> maṇikañcanācitaṃ, sovaṇṇajālacitaṃ mahantaṃ;
```

```
Abhiruyha gajavaraṃ sukappitaṃ, idhāgamā vehāyasaṃ <note>vehāsayaṃ (sī.)</note> antalikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§706.</p>

```
‘‘Nāgassa dantesu duvesu nimmitā, acchodakā <note>acchodikā (sī. ka.)</note> paduminiyo suphullā;
```

```
Padumesu ca turiyagaṇā pabhijjare, imā ca naccanti manoharāyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§707.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattāsi mahānubhāve, manussabhūtā kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§708.</p>

```
‘‘Bārāṇasiyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0072" /> upasaṅkamitvā, buddhassahaṃ vatthayugaṃ adāsiṃ;
```

```
Pādāni vanditvā <note>vanditva (sī.)</note> chamā nisīdiṃ, vittā cahaṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§709.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho ca me kañcanasannibhattaco, adesayi samudayadukkhaniccataṃ;
```

```
Asaṅkhataṃ dukkhanirodhasassataṃ, maggaṃ adesayi <note>adesesi (sī.)</note> yato vijānisaṃ;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§710.</p>

```
‘‘Appāyukī <pb ed="V" n="0.0045" /> kālakatā tato cutā, upapannā tidasagaṇaṃ yasassinī;
```

```
Sakkassahaṃ aññatarā pajāpati, yasuttarā nāma disāsu vissutā’’ti.
```

Nāgavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Alomavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§711.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="M" n="0.0059" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0060" /> vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§712.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…
```

```
Vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§714.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§715.</p>

```
‘‘Ahañca <pb ed="T" n="0.0073" /> bārāṇasiyaṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Adāsiṃ sukkhakummāsaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§716.</p>

```
‘‘Sukkhāya aloṇikāya ca, passa phalaṃ kummāsapiṇḍiyā;
```

```
Alomaṃ sukhitaṃ disvā, ko puññaṃ na karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§717.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… <pb ed="P" n="0.0061" /> vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Alomavimānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Kañjikadāyikāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§719.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena…pe… osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§720.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§722.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§723.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ andhakavindamhi, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Adāsiṃ kolasampākaṃ, kañjikaṃ teladhūpitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§724.</p>

```
‘‘Pipphalyā lasuṇena ca, missaṃ lāmañjakena ca;
```

```
Adāsiṃ ujubhūtasmiṃ <note>ujubhūtesu (ka.)</note>, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§725.</p>

```
‘‘Yā <pb ed="M" n="0.0060" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0046" /> mahesittaṃ kāreyya, cakkavattissa rājino;
```

```
Nārī sabbaṅgakalyāṇī, bhattu cānomadassikā;
```

```
Ekassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0074" /> kañjikadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§726.</p>

```
‘‘Sataṃ nikkhā sataṃ assā, sataṃ assatarīrathā;
```

```
Sataṃ kaññāsahassāni, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā;
```

```
Ekassa kañjikadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§727.</p>

```
‘‘Sataṃ hemavatā nāgā, īsādantā urūḷhavā;
```

```
Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā, hemakappanavāsasā;
```

```
Ekassa kañjikadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§728.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnamapi <pb ed="P" n="0.0062" /> dīpānaṃ, issaraṃ yodha kāraye;
```

```
Ekassa kañjikadānassa, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasi’’nti.
```

Kañjikadāyikāvimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Vihāravimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§729.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena…pe… osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§730.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
```

```
Dibbā saddā niccharanti, savanīyā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§731.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
```

```
Dibbā gandhā pavāyanti, sucigandhā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§732.</p>

```
‘‘Vivattamānā kāyena, yā veṇīsu piḷandhanā;
```

```
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, turiye pañcaṅgike yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§733.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṭaṃsakā vātadhutā, vātena sampakampitā;
```

```
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, turiye pañcaṅgike yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§734.</p>

```
‘‘Yāpi <pb ed="T" n="0.0075" /> te sirasmiṃ mālā, sucigandhā manoramā;
```

```
Vāti gandho disā sabbā, rukkho mañjūsako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§735.</p>

```
‘‘Ghāyase taṃ sucigandhaṃ, rūpaṃ passasi amānusaṃ;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§736.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvatthiyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0061" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0047" /> mayhaṃ sakhī bhadante, saṅghassa kāresi mahāvihāraṃ;
```

```
Tatthappasannā ahamānumodiṃ, disvā agārañca piyañca metaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§737.</p>

```
‘‘Tāyeva <pb ed="P" n="0.0063" /> me suddhanumodanāya, laddhaṃ vimānabbhutadassaneyyaṃ;
```

```
Samantato soḷasayojanāni, vehāyasaṃ gacchati iddhiyā mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§738.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārā nivesā me, vibhattā bhāgaso mitā;
```

<p rend="hangnum"></p>

```
Daddallamānā ābhanti, samantā satayojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§739.</p>

```
‘‘Pokkharañño ca me ettha, puthulomanisevitā;
```

```
Acchodakā <note>acchodikā (sī.)</note> vippasannā, soṇṇavālukasanthatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§740.</p>

```
‘‘Nānāpadumasañchannā, puṇḍarīkasamotatā <note>paṇḍarīkasamonatā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Surabhī sampavāyanti, manuññā māluteritā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§741.</p>

```
‘‘Jambuyo panasā tālā, nāḷikeravanāni ca;
```

```
Antonivesane jātā, nānārukkhā aropimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§742.</p>

```
‘‘Nānātūriyasaṅghuṭṭhaṃ<pb ed="T" n="0.0076" />, accharāgaṇaghositaṃ;
```

```
Yopi maṃ supine passe, sopi vitto siyā naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§743.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ abbhutadassaneyyaṃ, vimānaṃ sabbasopabhaṃ;
```

```
Mama kammehi nibbattaṃ, alaṃ puññāni kātave’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§744.</p>

```
‘‘Tāyeva te suddhanumodanāya, laddhaṃ vimānabbhutadassaneyyaṃ;
```

```
Yā ceva sā dānamadāsi nārī, tassā gatiṃ brūhi kuhiṃ uppannā <note>upapannā (ka.)</note> sā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§745.</p>

```
‘‘Yā sā ahu mayhaṃ sakhī bhadante, saṅghassa kāresi mahāvihāraṃ;
```

```
Viññātadhammā sā adāsi dānaṃ, uppannā nimmānaratīsu devesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§746.</p>

```
‘‘Pajāpatī <pb ed="M" n="0.0062" /> tassa sunimmitassa, acintiyā kammavipākā tassa;
```

```
Yametaṃ pucchasi kuhiṃ uppannā <note>upapannā (ka.)</note> sāti, taṃ te viyākāsiṃ anaññathā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§747.</p>

```
‘‘Tenahaññepi samādapetha, saṅghassa dānāni dadātha vittā;
```

```
Dhammañca suṇātha pasannamānasā, sudullabho laddho manussalābho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§748.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0077" /> maggaṃ maggādhipatī adesayi <note>maggādhipatyadesayi (sī.)</note>, brahmassaro kañcanasannibhattaco;
```

```
Saṅghassa dānāni dadātha vittā, mahapphalā yattha bhavanti dakkhiṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§749.</p>

```
<note>khu. pā. 6.6; su. ni. 229</note> ‘‘Ye <pb ed="P" n="0.0064" /> puggalā aṭṭha sataṃ pasatthā, cattāri etāni yugāni honti;
```

```
Te dakkhiṇeyyā sugatassa sāvakā, etesu dinnāni mahapphalāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§750.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 641</note> ‘‘Cattāro ca paṭipannā, cattāro ca phale ṭhitā;
```

```
Esa saṅgho ujubhūto, paññāsīlasamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§751.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 642</note> ‘‘Yajamānānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0048" /> manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§752.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 643</note> ‘‘Eso hi saṅgho vipulo mahaggato, esappameyyo udadhīva sāgaro;
```

```
Etehi seṭṭhā naravīrasāvakā, pabhaṅkarā dhammamudīrayanti <note>natthettha pāṭhabhedo</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§753.</p>

```
<note>vi. va. 644</note> ‘‘Tesaṃ sudinnaṃ suhutaṃ suyiṭṭhaṃ, ye saṅghamuddissa dadanti dānaṃ;
```

```
Sā dakkhiṇā saṅghagatā patiṭṭhitā, mahapphalā lokavidūna <note>lokavidūhi (ka.)</note> vaṇṇitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§754.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0078" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0063" /> yaññamanussarantā, ye vedajātā vicaranti loke;
```

```
Vineyya maccheramalaṃ samūlaṃ, aninditā saggamupenti ṭhāna’’nti.
```

Vihāravimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

Bhāṇavāraṃ dutiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 7. Caturitthivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§755.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="P" n="0.0065" /> vaṇṇena…pe…vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§758.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§759.</p>

```
‘‘Indīvarānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0066" /> hatthakaṃ ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa;
```

```
Esikānaṃ uṇṇatasmiṃ, nagaravare paṇṇakate ramme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§760.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadissā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§762.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena…pe…vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§765.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… <pb ed="T" n="0.0079" /> yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§766.</p>

```
‘‘Nīluppalahatthakaṃ ahamadāsiṃ, bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa;
```

```
Esikānaṃ uṇṇatasmiṃ, nagaravare paṇṇakate ramme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§767.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§769.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="M" n="0.0064" /> vaṇṇena…pe…vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§772.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§773.</p>

```
‘‘Odātamūlakaṃ haritapattaṃ, udakasmiṃ sare jātaṃ ahamadāsiṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa, esikānaṃ uṇṇatasmiṃ;
```

```
Nagaravare paṇṇakate ramme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§774.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§776.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="T" n="0.0080" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0049" /> vaṇṇena…pe…vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§779.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§780.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ sumanā sumanassa sumanamakuḷāni, dantavaṇṇāni ahamadāsiṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa, esikānaṃ uṇṇatasmiṃ;
```

```
Nagaravare paṇṇakate ramme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§781.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Caturitthivimānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Ambavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§783.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0067" /> te ambavanaṃ rammaṃ, pāsādettha mahallako;
```

```
Nānāturiyasaṅghuṭṭho, accharāgaṇaghosito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§784.</p>

```
‘‘Padīpo cettha jalati, niccaṃ sovaṇṇayo mahā;
```

```
Dussaphalehi rukkhehi, samantā parivārito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§785.</p>

```
‘‘Kena <pb ed="M" n="0.0065" /> tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§787.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… <pb ed="T" n="0.0081" /> yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§788.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, purimāya jātiyā manussaloke;
```

```
Vihāraṃ saṅghassa kāresiṃ, ambehi parivāritaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§789.</p>

```
‘‘Pariyosite vihāre, kārente niṭṭhite mahe;
```

```
Ambehi chādayitvāna <note>ambe acchādayitvāna (sī. syā.), ambehacchādayitvāna (pī. ka.)</note>, katvā dussamaye phale.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§790.</p>

```
‘‘Padīpaṃ tattha jāletvā, bhojayitvā gaṇuttamaṃ;
```

```
Niyyādesiṃ taṃ saṅghassa, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§791.</p>

```
‘‘Tena me ambavanaṃ rammaṃ, pāsādettha mahallako;
```

```
Nānāturiyasaṅghuṭṭho, accharāgaṇaghosito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§792.</p>

```
‘‘Padīpo <pb ed="P" n="0.0068" /> cettha jalati, niccaṃ sovaṇṇayo mahā;
```

```
Dussaphalehi rukkhehi, samantā parivārito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§793.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Ambavimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Pītavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§795.</p>

```
‘‘Pītavatthe <pb ed="V" n="0.0050" /> pītadhaje, pītālaṅkārabhūsite;
```

```
Pītacandanalittaṅge, pītauppalamālinī <note>pītuppalamadhārinī (syā. ka.), pītuppalamālinī (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§796.</p>

```
‘‘Pītapāsādasayane, pītāsane pītabhājane;
```

```
Pītachatte pītarathe, pītasse pītabījane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§797.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0082" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0066" /> kammamakarī bhadde, pubbe mānusake bhave;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§798.</p>

```
‘‘Kosātakī nāma latatthi bhante, tittikā anabhicchitā;
```

```
Tassā cattāri pupphāni, thūpaṃ abhihariṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§799.</p>

```
‘‘Satthu sarīramuddissa, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Nāssa maggaṃ avekkhissaṃ, na taggamanasā <note>tadaggamanasā (sī.), tadaṅgamanasā (syā.)</note> satī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§800.</p>

```
‘‘Tato maṃ avadhī gāvī, thūpaṃ apattamānasaṃ;
```

```
Tañcāhaṃ abhisañceyyaṃ, bhiyyo <note>bhīyo (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> nūna ito siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§801.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena devinda, maghavā devakuñjaro;
```

```
Pahāya mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tava sahabya <note>sahabyata (sī. syā.)</note> māgatā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§802.</p>

```
Idaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0069" /> sutvā tidasādhipati, maghavā devakuñjaro;
```

```
Tāvatiṃse pasādento, mātaliṃ etadabravi <note>etadabrūvīti (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§803.</p>

```
‘‘Passa mātali accheraṃ, cittaṃ kammaphalaṃ idaṃ;
```

```
Appakampi kataṃ deyyaṃ, puññaṃ hoti mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§804.</p>

```
‘‘Natthi citte pasannamhi, appakā nāma dakkhiṇā;
```

```
Tathāgate vā sambuddhe, atha vā tassa sāvake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§805.</p>

```
‘‘Ehi mātali amhepi, bhiyyo bhiyyo mahemase;
```

```
Tathāgatassa dhātuyo, sukho puññāna muccayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§806.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṭṭhante nibbute cāpi, same citte samaṃ phalaṃ;
```

```
Cetopaṇidhihetu <pb ed="T" n="0.0083" /> hi, sattā gacchanti suggatiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§807.</p>

```
‘‘Bahūnaṃ <note>bahunnaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> vata atthāya, uppajjanti tathāgatā;
```

```
Yattha kāraṃ karitvāna, saggaṃ gacchanti dāyakā’’ti.
```

Pītavimānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Ucchuvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§808.</p>

```
‘‘Obhāsayitvā <pb ed="M" n="0.0067" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0051" /> pathaviṃ sadevakaṃ, atirocasi candimasūriyā viya;
```

```
Siriyā ca vaṇṇena yasena tejasā, brahmāva deve tidase sahindake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§809.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="P" n="0.0070" /> taṃ uppalamāladhārinī, āveḷinī kañcanasannibhattace;
```

```
Alaṅkate uttamavatthadhārinī, kā tvaṃ subhe devate vandase mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§810.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure kammamakāsi attanā, manussabhūtā purimāya jātiyā;
```

```
Dānaṃ suciṇṇaṃ atha sīlasaññamaṃ, kenupapannā sugatiṃ yasassinī;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§811.</p>

```
‘‘Idāni bhante imameva gāmaṃ, piṇḍāya amhāka gharaṃ upāgami;
```

```
Tato te ucchussa adāsi khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacittā atulāya pītiyā;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§812.</p>

```
‘‘Sassu <pb ed="T" n="0.0084" /> ca pacchā anuyuñjate mamaṃ, kahaṃ nu ucchuṃ vadhuke avākirī;
```

```
Na chaḍḍitaṃ no pana khāditaṃ mayā, santassa bhikkhussa sayaṃ adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§813.</p>

```
‘‘Tuyhaṃnvidaṃ issariyaṃ atho mama, itissā sassu paribhāsate mamaṃ;
```

```
Leḍḍuṃ gahetvā pahāraṃ adāsi me, tato cutā kālakatāmhi devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§814.</p>

```
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
```

```
Devehi saddhiṃ paricārayāmahaṃ, modāmahaṃ kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§815.</p>

```
‘‘Tadeva <pb ed="M" n="0.0068" /> kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
```

```
Devindaguttā tidasehi rakkhitā, samappitā kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§816.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0085" /> puññaphalaṃ anappakaṃ, mahāvipākā mama ucchudakkhiṇā;
```

```
Devehi saddhiṃ paricārayāmahaṃ, modāmahaṃ kāmaguṇehi pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§817.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ puññaphalaṃ anappakaṃ, mahājutikā mama ucchudakkhiṇā;
```

```
Devindaguttā tidasehi rakkhitā, sahassanettoriva nandane vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§818.</p>

```
‘‘Tuvañca <pb ed="P" n="0.0071" /> bhante anukampakaṃ viduṃ, upecca vandiṃ kusalañca pucchisaṃ;
```

```
Tato te ucchussa adāsiṃ khaṇḍikaṃ, pasannacittā atulāya pītiyā’’ti.
```

Ucchuvimānaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 11. Vandanavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§819.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena <pb ed="V" n="0.0052" /> vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Obhāsentī disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§820.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe. <pb ed="P" n="0.0072" />…
```

```
Vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§822.</p>

```
Sā devatā attamanā…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§823.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā, disvāna samaṇe sīlavante;
```

```
Pādāni vanditvā manaṃ pasādayiṃ, vittā cahaṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§824.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="0.0069" /> metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="0.0086" /> ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Vandanavimānaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

#### 12. Rajjumālāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§826.</p>

```
‘‘Abhikkantena vaṇṇena, yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate;
```

```
Hatthapāde ca viggayha, naccasi suppavādite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§827.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
```

```
Dibbā saddā niccharanti, savanīyā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§828.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā te naccamānāya, aṅgamaṅgehi sabbaso;
```

```
Dibbā gandhā pavāyanti, sucigandhā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§829.</p>

```
‘‘Vivattamānā kāyena, yā veṇīsu piḷandhanā;
```

```
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, turiye pañcaṅgike yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§830.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṭaṃsakā vātadhutā, vātena sampakampitā;
```

```
Tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso, turiye pañcaṅgike yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§831.</p>

```
‘‘Yāpi te sirasmiṃ mālā, sucigandhā manoramā;
```

```
Vāti gandho disā sabbā, rukkho mañjūsako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§832.</p>

```
‘‘Ghāyase <pb ed="P" n="0.0073" /> taṃ sucigandhaṃ, rūpaṃ passasi amānusaṃ;
```

```
Devate pucchitācikkha, kissa kammassidaṃ phala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§833.</p>

```
‘‘Dāsī <pb ed="V" n="0.0053" /> ahaṃ pure āsiṃ, gayāyaṃ brāhmaṇassahaṃ;
```

```
Appapuññā alakkhikā, rajjumālāti maṃ viduṃ <note>vidū (syā. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§834.</p>

```
‘‘Akkosānaṃ vadhānañca, tajjanāya ca uggatā <note>ukkatā (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Kuṭaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0087" /> gahetvā nikkhamma, agañchiṃ <note>āgacchiṃ (syā. ka.), agacchiṃ (pī.), gacchiṃ (sī.)</note> udahāriyā <note>udakahāriyā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§835.</p>

```
‘‘Vipathe <pb ed="M" n="0.0070" /> kuṭaṃ nikkhipitvā, vanasaṇḍaṃ upāgamiṃ;
```

```
Idhevāhaṃ marissāmi, ko attho <note>kvatthosi (ka.), kīvatthopi (syā.)</note> jīvitena me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§836.</p>

```
‘‘Daḷhaṃ pāsaṃ karitvāna, āsumbhitvāna pādape;
```

```
Tato disā vilokesiṃ,ko nu kho vanamassito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§837.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, sabbalokahitaṃ muniṃ;
```

```
Nisinnaṃ rukkhamūlasmiṃ, jhāyantaṃ akutobhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§838.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā me ahu saṃvego, abbhuto lomahaṃsano;
```

```
Ko nu kho vanamassito, manusso udāhu devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§839.</p>

```
‘‘Pāsādikaṃ pasādanīyaṃ, vanā nibbanamāgataṃ;
```

```
Disvā mano me pasīdi, nāyaṃ yādisakīdiso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§840.</p>

```
‘‘Guttindriyo jhānarato, abahiggatamānaso;
```

```
Hito sabbassa lokassa, buddho ayaṃ <note>soyaṃ (sī.)</note> bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§841.</p>

```
‘‘Bhayabheravo durāsado, sīhova guhamassito;
```

```
Dullabhāyaṃ dassanāya, pupphaṃ odumbaraṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§842.</p>

```
‘‘So maṃ mudūhi vācāhi, ālapitvā tathāgato;
```

```
Rajjumāleti maṃvoca, saraṇaṃ gaccha tathāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§843.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ giraṃ suṇitvāna, nelaṃ atthavatiṃ suciṃ;
```

```
Saṇhaṃ muduñca vagguñca, sabbasokāpanūdanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§844.</p>

```
‘‘Kallacittañca maṃ ñatvā, pasannaṃ suddhamānasaṃ;
```

```
Hito <pb ed="T" n="0.0088" /> sabbassa lokassa, anusāsi tathāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§845.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ dukkhanti maṃvoca, ayaṃ dukkhassa sambhavo;
```

```
Dukkha <note>ayaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nirodho maggo ca <note>dukkhanirodho ca (syā.)</note>, añjaso amatogadho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§846.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampakassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0071" /> kusalassa, ovādamhi ahaṃ ṭhitā;
```

```
Ajjhagā amataṃ santiṃ, nibbānaṃ padamaccutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§847.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ avaṭṭhitāpemā, dassane avikampinī;
```

```
Mūlajātāya saddhāya, dhītā buddhassa orasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§848.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0054" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0074" /> ramāmi kīḷāmi, modāmi akutobhayā;
```

```
Dibbamālaṃ dhārayāmi, pivāmi madhumaddavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§849.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni, paṭibodhaṃ karonti me;
```

```
Āḷambo gaggaro bhīmo, sādhuvādī ca saṃsayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§850.</p>

```
‘‘Pokkharo ca suphasso ca, vīṇāmokkhā ca nāriyo;
```

```
Nandā ceva sunandā ca, soṇadinnā sucimhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§851.</p>

```
‘‘Alambusā missakesī ca, puṇḍarīkātidāruṇī <note>… ticāruṇī (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Eṇīphassā suphassā <note>supassā (syā. pī. ka.)</note> ca, subhaddā <note>saṃbhaddā (ka.)</note> muduvādinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§852.</p>

```
‘‘Etā caññā ca seyyāse, accharānaṃ pabodhikā;
```

```
Tā maṃ kālenupāgantvā, abhibhāsanti devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§853.</p>

```
‘‘Handa naccāma gāyāma, handa taṃ ramayāmase;
```

```
Nayidaṃ akatapuññānaṃ, katapuññānamevidaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§854.</p>

```
‘‘Asokaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0089" /> nandanaṃ rammaṃ, tidasānaṃ mahāvanaṃ;
```

```
Sukhaṃ akatapuññānaṃ, idha natthi parattha ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§855.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhañca katapuññānaṃ, idha ceva parattha ca;
```

```
Tesaṃ sahabyakāmānaṃ, kattabbaṃ kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Katapuññā hi modanti, sagge bhogasamaṅgino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§856.</p>

```
‘‘Bahūnaṃ vata atthāya, uppajjanti tathāgatā;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyā manussānaṃ, puññakhettānamākarā;
```

```
Yattha kāraṃ karitvāna, sagge modanti dāyakā’’ti.
```

Rajjumālāvimānaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

Mañjiṭṭhakavaggo catuttho niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0076" /> –

```
Mañjiṭṭhā <pb ed="M" n="0.0072" /> pabhassarā nāgā, alomākañjikadāyikā;
```

```
Vihāracaturitthambā, pītā ucchuvandanarajjumālā ca;
```

```
Vaggo tena pavuccatīti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Itthivimānaṃ samattaṃ.</trailer>

### 2. Purisavimānaṃ

#### 5. Mahārathavaggo

#### 1. Maṇḍūkadevaputtavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§857.</p>

```
‘‘Ko <pb ed="M" n="0.0073" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0055" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0077" /> me vandati pādāni, iddhiyā yasasā jalaṃ;
```

```
Abhikkantena vaṇṇena, sabbā obhāsayaṃ disā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§858.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍūkohaṃ pure āsiṃ, udake vārigocaro;
```

```
Tava dhammaṃ suṇantassa, avadhī vacchapālako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§859.</p>

```
‘‘Muhuttaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0090" /> cittapasādassa, iddhiṃ passa yasañca me;
```

```
Ānubhāvañca me passa, vaṇṇaṃ passa jutiñca me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§860.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca te dīghamaddhānaṃ, dhammaṃ assosuṃ gotama;
```

```
Pattā te acalaṭṭhānaṃ, yattha gantvā na socare’’ti.
```

Maṇḍūkadevaputtavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Revatīvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§861.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 219 dhammapade</note> ‘‘Cirappavāsiṃ purisaṃ, dūrato sotthimāgataṃ;
```

```
Ñātimittā suhajjā ca, abhinandanti āgataṃ;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§862.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 220 dhammapade</note> ‘‘Tatheva <pb ed="P" n="0.0078" /> katapuññampi, asmā lokā paraṃ gataṃ;
```

```
Puññāni paṭigaṇhanti, piyaṃ ñātīva āgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§863.</p>

```
<note>pe. va. 714</note>‘‘Uṭṭhehi revate supāpadhamme, apārutadvāre <note>apārubhaṃ dvāraṃ (sī. syā.), apārutadvāraṃ (pī. ka.)</note> adānasīle;
```

```
Nessāma taṃ yattha thunanti duggatā, samappitā nerayikā dukkhenā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§864.</p>

```
Icceva <pb ed="M" n="0.0074" /> <note>iccevaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> vatvāna yamassa dūtā, te dve yakkhā lohitakkhā brahantā;
```

```
Paccekabāhāsu gahetvā revataṃ, pakkāmayuṃ devagaṇassa santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§865.</p>

```
‘‘Ādiccavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0056" /> ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ, byamhaṃ subhaṃ kañcanajālachannaṃ;
```

```
Kassetamākiṇṇajanaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0091" /> vimānaṃ, sūriyassa raṃsīriva jotamānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§866.</p>

```
‘‘Nārīgaṇā candanasāralittā <note>candanasārānulittā (syā.)</note>, ubhato vimānaṃ upasobhayanti;
```

```
Taṃ dissati sūriyasamānavaṇṇaṃ, ko modati saggapatto vimāne’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§867.</p>

```
‘‘Bārāṇasiyaṃ nandiyo nāmāsi, upāsako amaccharī dānapati vadaññū;
```

```
Tassetamākiṇṇajanaṃ vimānaṃ, sūriyassa raṃsīriva jotamānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§868.</p>

```
‘‘Nārīgaṇā candanasāralittā, ubhato vimānaṃ upasobhayanti;
```

```
Taṃ dissati sūriyasamānavaṇṇaṃ, so modati saggapatto vimāne’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§869.</p>

```
‘‘Nandiyassāhaṃ bhariyā, agārinī sabbakulassa issarā;
```

```
Bhattu vimāne ramissāmi dānahaṃ, na patthaye nirayaṃ dassanāyā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§870.</p>

```
‘‘Eso te nirayo supāpadhamme, puññaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0092" /> tayā akataṃ jīvaloke;
```

```
Na hi maccharī rosako pāpadhammo, saggūpagānaṃ labhati sahabyata’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§871.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0075" /> nu gūthañca muttañca, asucī paṭidissati;
```

```
Duggandhaṃ kimidaṃ mīḷhaṃ, kimetaṃ upavāyatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§872.</p>

```
‘‘Esa saṃsavako nāma, gambhīro sataporiso;
```

```
Yattha vassasahassāni, tuvaṃ paccasi revate’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§873.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0079" /> nu kāyena vācāya, manasā dukkaṭaṃ kataṃ;
```

```
Kena saṃsavako laddho, gambhīro sataporiso’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§874.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi, aññe vāpi vanibbake <note>vaṇibbake (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Musāvādena vañcesi, taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§875.</p>

```
‘‘Tena saṃsavako laddho, gambhīro sataporiso;
```

```
Tattha vassasahassāni, tuvaṃ paccasi revate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§876.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthepi chindanti athopi pāde, kaṇṇepi chindanti athopi nāsaṃ;
```

```
Athopi kākoḷagaṇā samecca, saṅgamma khādanti viphandamāna’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§877.</p>

```
‘‘Sādhu kho maṃ paṭinetha, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Dānena samacariyāya, saṃyamena damena ca;
```

```
Yaṃ katvā sukhitā honti, na ca pacchānutappare’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§878.</p>

```
‘‘Pure <pb ed="T" n="0.0093" /> tuvaṃ pamajjitvā, idāni paridevasi;
```

```
Sayaṃ katānaṃ kammānaṃ, vipākaṃ anubhossasī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§879.</p>

```
‘‘Ko <pb ed="V" n="0.0057" /> devalokato manussalokaṃ, gantvāna puṭṭho me evaṃ vadeyya;
```

```
‘Nikkhittadaṇḍesu dadātha dānaṃ, acchādanaṃ seyya <note>sayana (sī.)</note> mathannapānaṃ;
```

```
Nahi maccharī rosako pāpadhammo, saggūpagānaṃ labhati sahabyataṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§880.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ nūna ito gantvā, yoniṃ laddhāna mānusiṃ;
```

```
Vadaññū sīlasampannā, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Dānena samacariyāya, saṃyamena damena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§881.</p>

```
‘‘Ārāmāni <pb ed="M" n="0.0076" /> ca ropissaṃ, dugge saṅkamanāni ca;
```

```
Papañca udapānañca, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§882.</p>

```
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§883.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā;
```

```
Na ca dāne pamajjissaṃ, sāmaṃ diṭṭhamidaṃ mayā’’ti;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§884.</p>

```
Iccevaṃ vippalapantiṃ, phandamānaṃ tato tato;
```

```
Khipiṃsu niraye ghore, uddhapādaṃ avaṃsiraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§885.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ pure maccharinī ahosiṃ, paribhāsikā <pb ed="T" n="0.0094" /> samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ;
```

```
Vitathena ca sāmikaṃ vañcayitvā, paccāmahaṃ niraye ghorarūpe’’ti.
```

Revatīvimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Chattamāṇavakavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§886.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="P" n="0.0080" /> vadataṃ pavaro manujesu, sakyamunī bhagavā katakicco;
```

```
Pāragato balavīriyasamaṅgī <note>balavīrasamaṅgī (ka.)</note>, taṃ sugataṃ saraṇatthamupehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§887.</p>

```
‘‘Rāgavirāgamanejamasokaṃ, dhammamasaṅkhatamappaṭikūlaṃ;
```

```
Madhuramimaṃ paguṇaṃ suvibhattaṃ, dhammamimaṃ saraṇatthamupehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§888.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha <pb ed="P" n="0.0081" /> ca dinna mahapphalamāhu, catūsu sucīsu purisayugesu;
```

```
Aṭṭha ca puggaladhammadasā te, saṅghamimaṃ saraṇatthamupehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§889.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="0.0077" /> tathā tapati nabhe sūriyo, cando ca na bhāsati na phusso;
```

```
Yathā atulamidaṃ mahappabhāsaṃ, ko <pb ed="T" n="0.0095" /> nu tvaṃ tidivā mahiṃ upāgā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§890.</p>

```
‘‘Chindati <pb ed="V" n="0.0058" /> raṃsī pabhaṅkarassa, sādhikavīsatiyojanāni ābhā;
```

```
Rattimapi yathā divaṃ karoti, parisuddhaṃ vimalaṃ subhaṃ vimānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§891.</p>

```
‘‘Bahupadumavicitrapuṇḍarīkaṃ, vokiṇṇaṃ kusumehi nekacittaṃ;
```

```
Arajavirajahemajālachannaṃ, ākāse tapati yathāpi sūriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§892.</p>

```
‘‘Rattambarapītavasasāhi, agarupiyaṅgucandanussadāhi;
```

```
Kañcanatanusannibhattacāhi, paripūraṃ gaganaṃva tārakāhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§893.</p>

```
‘‘Naranāriyo <note>naranārī (ka.), nāriyo (?)</note> bahuketthanekavaṇṇā, kusumavibhūsitābharaṇettha sumanā;
```

```
Anilapamuñcitā pavanti <note>pavāyanti (ka.)</note> surabhiṃ, tapaniyavitatā suvaṇṇachannā <note>suvaṇṇacchādanā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§894.</p>

```
‘‘Kissa saṃyamassa <note>samadamassa (sī.)</note> ayaṃ vipāko, kenāsi kammaphalenidhūpapanno;
```

```
Yathā <pb ed="T" n="0.0096" /> ca te adhigatamidaṃ vimānaṃ, tadanupadaṃ avacāsi iṅgha puṭṭho’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§895.</p>

```
‘‘Sayamidha <note>yamidha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pathe samecca māṇavena, satthānusāsi anukampamāno;
```

```
Tava ratanavarassa dhammaṃ sutvā, karissāmīti ca bravittha chatto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§896.</p>

```
‘‘Jinavarapavaraṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0078" /> <note>jinapavaraṃ (syā. ka.)</note> upehi <note>upemi (bahūsu)</note> saraṇaṃ, dhammañcāpi tatheva bhikkhusaṅghaṃ;
```

```
Noti paṭhamaṃ avocahaṃ <note>avocāhaṃ (sī. syā. ka.)</note> bhante, pacchā te vacanaṃ tathevakāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§897.</p>

```
‘‘Mā ca pāṇavadhaṃ vividhaṃ carassu asuciṃ,
```

```
Na hi pāṇesu asaññataṃ avaṇṇayiṃsu sappaññā;
```

```
Noti paṭhamaṃ avocahaṃ bhante,
```

```
Pacchā te vacanaṃ tathevakāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§898.</p>

```
‘‘Mā <pb ed="P" n="0.0082" /> ca parajanassa rakkhitampi, ādātabbamamaññitho <note>mamaññittha (sī. pī.)</note> adinnaṃ;
```

```
Noti paṭhamaṃ avocahaṃ bhante, pacchā vacanaṃ tathevakāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§899.</p>

```
‘‘Mā ca parajanassa rakkhitāyo, parabhariyā agamā anariyametaṃ;
```

```
Noti paṭhamaṃ avocahaṃ bhante, pacchā te vacanaṃ tathevakāsiṃ;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§900.</p>

```
‘‘Mā ca vitathaṃ aññathā abhāṇi,
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0097" /> hi musāvādaṃ avaṇṇayiṃsu sappaññā;
```

```
Noti paṭhamaṃ avocahaṃ bhante, pacchā te vacanaṃ tathevakāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§901.</p>

```
‘‘Yena ca purisassa apeti saññā, taṃ majjaṃ parivajjayassu sabbaṃ;
```

```
Noti paṭhamaṃ avocahaṃ bhante, pacchā te vacanaṃ tathevakāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§902.</p>

```
‘‘Svāhaṃ idha pañca sikkhā karitvā, paṭipajjitvā tathāgatassa dhamme;
```

```
Dvepathamagamāsiṃ coramajjhe, te maṃ tattha vadhiṃsu bhogahetu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§903.</p>

```
‘‘Ettakamidaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0079" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0059" /> anussarāmi kusalaṃ, tato paraṃ na me vijjati aññaṃ;
```

```
Tena sucaritena kammunāhaṃ <note>kammanāhaṃ (sī.)</note>, uppanno <note>upapanno (bahūsu)</note> tidivesu kāmakāmī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§904.</p>

```
‘‘Passa khaṇamuhuttasaññamassa, anudhammappaṭipattiyā vipākaṃ;
```

```
Jalamiva yasasā samekkhamānā, bahukā maṃ pihayanti hīnakammā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§905.</p>

```
‘‘Passa katipayāya desanāya, sugatiñcamhi <pb ed="T" n="0.0098" /> gato sukhañca patto;
```

```
Ye ca te satataṃ suṇanti dhammaṃ, maññe te amataṃ phusanti khemaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§906.</p>

```
‘‘Appampi kataṃ mahāvipākaṃ, vipulaṃ hoti <note>vipulaphalaṃ (ka.)</note> tathāgatassa dhamme;
```

```
Passa katapuññatāya chatto, obhāseti pathaviṃ yathāpi sūriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§907.</p>

```
‘‘Kimidaṃ kusalaṃ kimācarema, icceke hi samecca mantayanti;
```

```
Te mayaṃ punareva <note>punapi (?)</note> laddha mānusattaṃ, paṭipannā viharemu sīlavanto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§908.</p>

```
‘‘Bahukāro <pb ed="P" n="0.0083" /> anukampako ca satthā, iti me sati agamā divā divassa;
```

```
Svāhaṃ upagatomhi saccanāmaṃ, anukampassu punapi suṇemu <note>suṇoma (sī.), suṇomi (syā.)</note> dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§909.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="M" n="0.0080" /> cidha <note>yedha (sī. syā. pī.), ye idha (ka.)</note> pajahanti kāmarāgaṃ, bhavarāgānusayañca pahāya mohaṃ;
```

```
Na ca te punamupenti gabbhaseyyaṃ, parinibbānagatā hi sītibhūtā’’ti.
```

Chattamāṇavakavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Kakkaṭakarasadāyakavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§910.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0099" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0084" /> maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā <note>ruciratthatā (syā. ka.) 646 gāthāyaṃ ‘‘rucakupakiṇṇaṃ’’ti padassa saṃvaṇṇanā passitabbā</note> subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§911.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi <pb ed="P" n="0.0085" /> pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ <note>vaggu (sī. ka.), vaggū (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§912.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§913.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ deva mahānubhāva, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§914.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§915.</p>

```
‘‘Satisamuppādakaro<pb ed="V" n="0.0060" />, dvāre kakkaṭako ṭhito;
```

```
Niṭṭhito jātarūpassa, sobhati dasapādako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§916.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="0.0081" /> metādiso vaṇṇo, tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti <pb ed="T" n="0.0100" /> ca me bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§917.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva, manussabhūto yamakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Kakkaṭakarasadāyakavimānaṃ catutthaṃ.

(Anantaraṃ pañcavimānaṃ yathā kakkaṭakarasadāyakavimānaṃ tathā vitthāretabbaṃ)

#### 5. Dvārapālavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§918.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0086" /> maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§919.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§920.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe… <pb ed="T" n="0.0101" /> vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§922.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§923.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbaṃ mamaṃ vassasahassamāyu, vācābhigītaṃ manasā pavattitaṃ;
```

```
Ettāvatā ṭhassati puññakammo, dibbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§924.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="0.0082" /> metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dvārapālavimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Paṭhamakaraṇīyavimānavatthu


```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§927.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi <pb ed="V" n="0.0061" /> pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§928.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…
```

```
Vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§930.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe…yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§931.</p>

```
‘‘Karaṇīyāni puññāni, paṇḍitena vijānatā;
```

```
Sammaggatesu buddhesu, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§932.</p>

```
‘‘Atthāya vata me buddho, araññā gāmamāgato;
```

```
Tattha <pb ed="T" n="0.0102" /> cittaṃ pasādetvā, tāvatiṃsūpago ahaṃ <note>ahuṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§933.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamakaraṇīyavimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

#### 8. Paṭhamasūcivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§944.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0062" /> maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§945.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi <pb ed="M" n="0.0084" /> pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§946.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§948.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="0.0103" /> devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§949.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ dadāti na taṃ hoti,
```

```
Yañceva dajjā tañceva seyyo;
```

```
Sūci dinnā sūcimeva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§950.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamasūcivimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Dutiyasūcivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§952.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§953.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§954.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="0.0104" /> ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§956.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§957.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto,purimajātiyā manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§958.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0085" /> virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ;
```

```
Tassa adāsahaṃ sūciṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§959.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dutiyasūcivimānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Paṭhamanāgavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§961.</p>

```
‘‘Susukkakhandhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0063" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0088" /> abhiruyha nāgaṃ, akācinaṃ dantiṃ baliṃ mahājavaṃ;
```

```
Abhiruyha gajavaraṃ <note>gajaṃ varaṃ (syā.)</note> sukappitaṃ, idhāgamā vehāyasaṃ antalikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§962.</p>

```
‘‘Nāgassa dantesu duvesu nimmitā, acchodakā paduminiyo suphullā;
```

```
Padumesu ca turiyagaṇā pavajjare, imā ca naccanti manoharāyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§963.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§964.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§965.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭheva muttapupphāni, kassapassa mahesino <note>bhagavato (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Thūpasmiṃ abhiropesiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§966.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamanāgavimānaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 11. Dutiyanāgavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§968.</p>

```
‘‘Mahantaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0086" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0089" /> nāgaṃ abhiruyha, sabbasetaṃ gajuttamaṃ;
```

```
Vanā vanaṃ anupariyāsi, nārīgaṇapurakkhato;
```

```
Obhāsento disā sabbā, osadhī viya tārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§969.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§971.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano, vaṅgīseneva pucchito;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§972.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, upāsako cakkhumato ahosiṃ;
```

```
Pāṇātipātā virato ahosiṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§973.</p>

```
‘‘Amajjapo <pb ed="T" n="0.0105" /> no ca musā abhāṇiṃ <note>abhāsiṃ (sī. ka.)</note>, sakena dārena ca tuṭṭho ahosiṃ;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacitto, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§974.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Dutiyanāgavimānaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

#### 12. Tatiyanāgavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§976.</p>

```
‘‘Ko <pb ed="V" n="0.0064" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0090" /> nu dibbena yānena, sabbasetena hatthinā;
```

```
Turiyatāḷitanigghoso, antalikkhe mahīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§977.</p>

```
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu <note>ādu (sī. syā.)</note> sakko purindado;
```

```
Ajānantā taṃ pucchāma, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§978.</p>

```
‘‘Namhi <pb ed="M" n="0.0087" /> devo na gandhabbo, nāpi <note>nāmhi (ka.)</note> sakko purindado;
```

```
Sudhammā nāma ye devā, tesaṃ aññataro aha’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§979.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāma devaṃ sudhammaṃ <note>deva sudhamma (syā.), deva sudhammaṃ (ka.)</note>, puthuṃ katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Kiṃ katvā mānuse kammaṃ, sudhammaṃ upapajjatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§980.</p>

```
‘‘Ucchāgāraṃ tiṇāgāraṃ, vatthāgārañca yo dade;
```

```
Tiṇṇaṃ aññataraṃ datvā, sudhammaṃ upapajjatī’’ti.
```

Tatiyanāgavimānaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

#### 13. Cūḷarathavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§981.</p>

```
‘‘Daḷhadhammā nisārassa, dhanuṃ olubbha tiṭṭhasi;
```

```
Khattiyo nusi rājañño, adu luddo vanecaro’’ti <note>vanācaroti (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§982.</p>

```
‘‘Assakādhipatissāhaṃ<pb ed="T" n="0.0106" />, bhante putto vanecaro;
```

```
Nāmaṃ me bhikkhu te brūmi, sujāto iti maṃ vidū <note>viduṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§983.</p>

```
‘‘Mige gavesamānohaṃ, ogāhanto brahāvanaṃ;
```

```
Migaṃ tañceva <note>migaṃ gantveva (syā.), migavadhañca (ka.)</note> nāddakkhiṃ, tañca disvā ṭhito aha’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§984.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0091" /> te mahāpuñña, atho te adurāgataṃ;
```

```
Etto udakamādāya, pāde pakkhālayassu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§985.</p>

```
‘‘Idampi pānīyaṃ sītaṃ, ābhataṃ girigabbharā;
```

```
Rājaputta tato pitvā <note>pītvā (sī. syā.)</note>, santhatasmiṃ upāvisā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§986.</p>

```
‘‘Kalyāṇī vata te vācā, savanīyā mahāmuni;
```

```
Nelā atthavatī <note>catthavatī (sī.)</note> vaggu, mantvā <note>mantā (syā. pī. ka.)</note> atthañca bhāsasi <note>bhāsase (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§987.</p>

```
‘‘Kā <pb ed="V" n="0.0065" /> te rati vane viharato, isinisabha vadehi puṭṭho;
```

```
Tava vacanapathaṃ nisāmayitvā, atthadhammapadaṃ samācaremase’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§988.</p>

```
‘‘Ahiṃsā <pb ed="M" n="0.0088" /> sabbapāṇīnaṃ, kumāramhāka ruccati;
```

```
Theyyā ca aticārā ca, majjapānā ca ārati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§989.</p>

```
‘‘Ārati samacariyā ca, bāhusaccaṃ kataññutā;
```

```
Diṭṭheva dhamme pāsaṃsā, dhammā ete pasaṃsiyāti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§990.</p>

```
‘‘Santike maraṇaṃ tuyhaṃ, oraṃ māsehi pañcahi;
```

```
Rājaputta <pb ed="T" n="0.0107" /> vijānāhi, attānaṃ parimocayā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§991.</p>

```
‘‘Katamaṃ svāhaṃ janapadaṃ gantvā, kiṃ kammaṃ kiñca porisaṃ;
```

```
Kāya vā pana vijjāya, bhaveyyaṃ ajarāmaro’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§992.</p>

```
‘‘Na vijjate so padeso, kammaṃ vijjā ca porisaṃ;
```

```
Yattha gantvā bhave macco, rājaputtājarāmaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§993.</p>

```
‘‘Mahaddhanā mahābhogā, raṭṭhavantopi khattiyā;
```

```
Pahūtadhanadhaññāse, tepi no <note>tepi na (bahūsu)</note> ajarāmarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§994.</p>

```
‘‘Yadi te sutā andhakaveṇḍuputtā <note>andhakaveṇhuputtā (sī.), aṇḍakaveṇḍaputtā (syā. ka.)</note>, sūrā vīrā vikkantappahārino;
```

```
Tepi āyukkhayaṃ pattā, viddhastā sassatīsamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§995.</p>

```
‘‘Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
```

```
Ete caññe ca jātiyā, tepi no ajarāmarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§996.</p>

```
‘‘Ye mantaṃ parivattenti, chaḷaṅgaṃ brahmacintitaṃ;
```

```
Ete caññe ca vijjāya, tepi no ajarāmarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§997.</p>

```
‘‘Isayo cāpi ye santā, saññatattā tapassino;
```

```
Sarīraṃ tepi kālena, vijahanti tapassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§998.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāvitattāpi <pb ed="P" n="0.0092" /> arahanto, katakiccā anāsavā;
```

```
Nikkhipanti imaṃ dehaṃ, puññapāpaparikkhayā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§999.</p>

```
‘‘Subhāsitā atthavatī, gāthāyo te mahāmuni;
```

```
Nijjhattomhi <pb ed="T" n="0.0108" /> subhaṭṭhena, tvañca me saraṇaṃ bhavā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1000.</p>

```
‘‘Mā <pb ed="M" n="0.0089" /> maṃ tvaṃ saraṇaṃ gaccha, tameva saraṇaṃ vaja <note>bhaja (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sakyaputtaṃ mahāvīraṃ, yamahaṃ saraṇaṃ gato’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1001.</p>

```
‘‘Katarasmiṃ so janapade, satthā tumhāka mārisa;
```

```
Ahampi daṭṭhuṃ gacchissaṃ, jinaṃ appaṭipuggala’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1002.</p>

```
‘‘Puratthimasmiṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0066" /> janapade, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Tatthāsi purisājañño, so ca kho parinibbuto’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1003.</p>

```
‘‘Sace hi buddho tiṭṭheyya, satthā tumhāka mārisa;
```

```
Yojanāni sahassāni, gaccheyyaṃ <note>gacche (syā. pī. ka.)</note> payirupāsituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1004.</p>

```
‘‘Yato ca kho <note>yatā kho (pī. ka.)</note> parinibbuto, satthā tumhāka mārisa;
```

```
Nibbutampi <note>parinibbutaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> mahāvīraṃ, gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1005.</p>

```
‘‘Upemi saraṇaṃ buddhaṃ, dhammañcāpi anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Saṅghañca naradevassa, gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1006.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viramāmi khippaṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayāmi;
```

```
Amajjapo no ca musā bhaṇāmi, sakena dārena ca homi tuṭṭho’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1007.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassaraṃsīva yathā mahappabho, disaṃ yathā bhāti nabhe anukkamaṃ;
```

```
Tathāpakāro <note>tathappakāro (sī. syā.)</note> tavāyaṃ <note>tavayaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> mahāratho, samantato <pb ed="T" n="0.0109" /> yojanasattamāyato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1008.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇapaṭṭehi samantamotthaṭo, urassa muttāhi maṇīhi cittito;
```

```
Lekhā suvaṇṇassa ca rūpiyassa ca, sobhenti veḷuriyamayā sunimmitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1009.</p>

```
‘‘Sīsañcidaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0090" /> veḷuriyassa nimmitaṃ, yugañcidaṃ lohitakāya cittitaṃ;
```

```
Yuttā suvaṇṇassa ca rūpiyassa ca, sobhanti assā ca ime manojavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1010.</p>

```
‘‘So tiṭṭhasi hemarathe adhiṭṭhito, devānamindova sahassavāhano;
```

```
Pucchāmi tāhaṃ yasavanta kovidaṃ <note>kovida (ka.)</note>, kathaṃ tayā laddho ayaṃ uḷāro’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1011.</p>

```
‘‘Sujāto <pb ed="P" n="0.0093" /> nāmahaṃ bhante, rājaputto pure ahuṃ;
```

```
Tvañca maṃ anukampāya, saññamasmiṃ nivesayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1012.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇāyukañca maṃ ñatvā, sarīraṃ pādāsi satthuno;
```

```
Imaṃ sujāta pūjehi, taṃ te atthāya hehiti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1013.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ gandhehi mālehi, pūjayitvā samuyyuto;
```

```
Pahāya mānusaṃ dehaṃ, upapannomhi nandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1014.</p>

```
‘‘Nandane <pb ed="T" n="0.0110" /> ca vane <note>nandanopavane (sī.), nandane pavane (syā. ka.)</note> ramme, nānādijagaṇāyute;
```

```
Ramāmi naccagītehi, accharāhi purakkhato’’ti.
```

Cūḷarathavimānaṃ terasamaṃ.

#### 14. Mahārathavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1015.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassayuttaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0067" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0094" /> hayavāhanaṃ subhaṃ, āruyhimaṃ sandanaṃ nekacittaṃ;
```

```
Uyyānabhūmiṃ abhito anukkamaṃ, purindado bhūtapatīva vāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1016.</p>

```
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayā te rathakubbarā ubho, phalehi <note>thalehi (sī.)</note> aṃsehi atīva saṅgatā;
```

```
Sujātagumbā naravīraniṭṭhitā, virocatī pannaraseva cando.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1017.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇajālāvatato <pb ed="M" n="0.0091" /> ratho ayaṃ, bahūhi nānāratanehi cittito;
```

```
Sunandighoso ca subhassaro ca, virocatī cāmarahatthabāhubhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1018.</p>

```
‘‘Imā ca nābhyo manasābhinimmitā, rathassa pādantaramajjhabhūsitā;
```

```
Imā ca nābhyo satarājicittitā, sateratā vijjurivappabhāsare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1019.</p>

```
‘‘Anekacittāvatato <pb ed="T" n="0.0111" /> ratho ayaṃ, puthū ca nemī ca sahassaraṃsiko;
```

```
Tesaṃ saro suyyati <note>sūyati (sī.)</note> vaggurūpo, pañcaṅgikaṃ turiyamivappavāditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1020.</p>

```
‘‘Sirasmiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0095" /> cittaṃ maṇicandakappitaṃ, sadā visuddhaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ;
```

```
Suvaṇṇarājīhi atīva saṅgataṃ, veḷuriyarājīva atīva sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1021.</p>

```
‘‘Ime ca vāḷī maṇicandakappitā, ārohakambū sujavā brahūpamā.
```

```
Brahā mahantā balino mahājavā, mano tavaññāya tatheva siṃsare <note>sabbare (ka.), sappare (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1022.</p>

```
‘‘Ime ca sabbe sahitā catukkamā, mano tavaññāya tatheva siṃsare;
```

```
Samaṃ vahantā mudukā anuddhatā, āmodamānā turagāna <note>turaṅgāna (ka.)</note> muttamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1023.</p>

```
‘‘Dhunanti vagganti patanti <note>pavattanti (pī. ka.)</note> cambare, abbhuddhunantā sukate piḷandhane;
```

```
Tesaṃ saro suyyati vaggurūpo, pañcaṅgikaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0112" /> turiyamivappavāditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1024.</p>

```
‘‘Rathassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0092" /> ghoso apiḷandhanāna ca, khurassa nādo <note>nādī (syā.), nādi (pī. ka.)</note> abhihiṃsanāya ca;
```

```
Ghoso suvaggū samitassa suyyati, gandhabbatūriyāni vicitrasaṃvane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1025.</p>

```
‘‘Rathe ṭhitā tā migamandalocanā, āḷārapamhā hasitā piyaṃvadā;
```

```
Veḷuriyajālāvatatā tanucchavā, sadeva gandhabbasūraggapūjitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1026.</p>

```
‘‘Tā rattarattambarapītavāsasā, visālanettā abhirattalocanā;
```

```
Kule sujātā sutanū sucimhitā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1027.</p>

```
‘‘Tā kambukeyūradharā suvāsasā, sumajjhimā ūruthanūpapannā;
```

```
Vaṭṭaṅguliyo sumukhā sudassanā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1028.</p>

```
‘‘Aññā suveṇī susu missakesiyo, samaṃ vibhattāhi pabhassarāhi ca;
```

```
Anubbatā tā tava mānase ratā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1029.</p>

```
‘‘Āveḷiniyo <pb ed="V" n="0.0068" /> padumuppalacchadā, alaṅkatā candanasāravāsitā <note>vositā (syā.), bhūsitā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Anubbatā <pb ed="T" n="0.0113" /> tā tava mānase ratā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1030.</p>

```
‘‘Tā <pb ed="P" n="0.0096" /> māliniyo padumuppalacchadā, alaṅkatā candanasāravāsitā;
```

```
Anubbatā tā tava mānase ratā, rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1031.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇṭhesu <pb ed="M" n="0.0093" /> te yāni piḷandhanāni, hatthesu pādesu tatheva sīse;
```

```
Obhāsayantī dasa sabbaso disā, abbhuddayaṃ sāradikova bhāṇumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1032.</p>

```
‘‘Vātassa vegena ca sampakampitā, bhujesu mālā apiḷandhanāni ca;
```

```
Muñcanti ghosaṃ rūciraṃ suciṃ subhaṃ, sabbehi viññūhi sutabbarūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1033.</p>

```
‘‘Uyyānabhūmyā ca duvaddhato ṭhitā, rathā <pb ed="T" n="0.0114" /> ca nāgā tūriyāni ca saro;
```

```
Tameva devinda pamodayanti, vīṇā yathā pokkharapattabāhubhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1034.</p>

```
‘‘Imāsu vīṇāsu bahūsu vaggūsu, manuññarūpāsu hadayeritaṃ pītiṃ <note>hadayeritaṃ pati (sī.), hadayeritampi taṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Pavajjamānāsu atīva accharā, bhamanti kaññā padumesu sikkhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1035.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā ca gītāni ca vāditāni ca, naccāni cimāni <note>cemāni (sī.)</note> samenti ekato;
```

```
Athettha naccanti athettha accharā, obhāsayantī ubhato varitthiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1036.</p>

```
‘‘So modasi turiyagaṇappabodhano, mahīyamāno vajirāvudhoriva;
```

```
Imāsu vīṇāsu bahūsu vaggūsu, manuññarūpāsu hadayeritaṃ pītiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1037.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ tvaṃ pure kammamakāsi attanā, manussabhūto purimāya jātiyā;
```

```
Uposathaṃ kaṃ vā <note>uposathaṃ kiṃ va (syā.)</note> tuvaṃ upāvasi, kaṃ <note>kiṃ (syā.)</note> dhammacariyaṃ vatamābhirocayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1038.</p>

```
‘‘Nayīdamappassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0094" /> katassa <note>nayidaṃ appassa katassa (sī. syā.), sāsedaṃ appakatassa (ka.)</note> kammuno, pubbe suciṇṇassa uposathassa vā;
```

```
Iddhānubhāvo <pb ed="T" n="0.0115" /> vipulo ayaṃ tava, yaṃ devasaṅghaṃ abhirocase bhusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1039.</p>

```
‘‘Dānassa te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
```

```
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1040.</p>

```
So <pb ed="P" n="0.0097" /> devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1041.</p>

```
‘‘Jitindriyaṃ buddhamanomanikkamaṃ, naruttamaṃ kassapamaggapuggalaṃ;
```

```
Avāpurantaṃ amatassa dvāraṃ, devātidevaṃ satapuññalakkhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1042.</p>

```
‘‘Tamaddasaṃ kuñjaramoghatiṇṇaṃ, suvaṇṇasiṅgīnadabimbasādisaṃ;
```

```
Disvāna taṃ khippamahuṃ sucīmano, tameva disvāna subhāsitaddhajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1043.</p>

```
‘‘Tamannapānaṃ athavāpi cīvaraṃ, suciṃ paṇītaṃ rasasā upetaṃ;
```

```
Pupphābhikkiṇamhi sake nivesane, patiṭṭhapesiṃ sa asaṅgamānaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1044.</p>

```
‘‘Tamannapānena <pb ed="V" n="0.0069" /> ca cīvarena ca, khajjena bhojjena ca sāyanena ca;
```

```
Santappayitvā <pb ed="T" n="0.0116" /> dvipadānamuttamaṃ, so saggaso devapure ramāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1045.</p>

```

```

‘‘Etenupāyena imaṃ niraggaḷaṃ, yaññaṃ yajitvā tividhaṃ visuddhaṃ.

```
Pahāyahaṃ mānusakaṃ samussayaṃ, indūpamo <note>indassamo (syā. ka.)</note> devapure ramāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1046.</p>

```
‘‘Āyuñca <pb ed="M" n="0.0095" /> vaṇṇañca sukhaṃ balañca, paṇītarūpaṃ abhikaṅkhatā muni;
```

```
Annañca pānañca bahuṃ susaṅkhataṃ, patiṭṭhapetabbamasaṅgamānase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1047.</p>

```
<note>kathā. 799</note>‘‘Nayimasmiṃ loke parasmiṃ <note>nayimasmiṃ vā loke parasmiṃ (kathāvatthu 799), nayimasmi loke va parasmi (?)</note> vā pana, buddhena seṭṭho va samo va vijjati;
```

```
Āhuneyyānaṃ <note>yamāhuneyyānaṃ (ka.)</note> paramāhutiṃ gato, puññatthikānaṃ vipulapphalesina’’nti.
```

Mahārathavimānaṃ cuddasamaṃ.

Mahārathavaggo pañcamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0100" /> –

```
Maṇḍūko revatī chatto, kakkaṭo dvārapālako;
```

```
Dve karaṇīyā dve sūci, tayo nāgā ca dve rathā;
```

```
Purisānaṃ paṭhamo vaggo pavuccatīti.
```

Bhāṇavāraṃ tatiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 6. Pāyāsivaggo

#### 1. Paṭhamaagāriyavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1048.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="T" n="0.0117" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0070" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0101" /> vanaṃ cittalataṃ pabhāsati <note>pakāsati (ka.)</note>, uyyānaseṭṭhaṃ tidasānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Tathūpamaṃ tuyhamidaṃ vimānaṃ, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1049.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1050.</p>

```
So <pb ed="M" n="0.0096" /> devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1051.</p>

```
‘‘Ahañca bhariyā ca manussaloke, opānabhūtā gharamāvasimha;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacittā, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adamha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1052.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamaagāriyavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 3. Phaladāyakavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1060.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0071" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0097" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0103" /> maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato soḷasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1061.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā <pb ed="T" n="0.0119" /> ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Aṭṭhaṭṭhakā sikkhitā sādhurūpā, dibbā ca kaññā tidasacarā uḷārā;
```

```
Naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1062.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1063.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1064.</p>

```
‘‘Phaladāyī phalaṃ vipulaṃ labhati, dadamujugatesu pasannamānaso;
```

```
So hi pamodati <note>modati (sī. syā. pī.)</note> saggagato tidive <note>tattha (ka.)</note>, anubhoti ca puññaphalaṃ vipulaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1065.</p>

```
‘‘Tavevāhaṃ <note>tathevāhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mahāmuni, adāsiṃ caturo phale.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1066.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā hi phalaṃ alameva dātuṃ, niccaṃ manussena sukhatthikena;
```

```
Dibbāni vā patthayatā sukhāni, manussasobhaggatamicchatā vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1067.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="0.0120" /> metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…
```

```
Vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Phaladāyakavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0073" /> manussesu manussabhūto, ahosiṃ yavapālako;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ, vippasannamanāvilaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1091.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0107" /> adāsahaṃ bhāgaṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Kummāsapiṇḍaṃ datvāna, modāmi nandane vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1092.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="0.0100" /> metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Yavapālakavimānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Paṭhamakuṇḍalīvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1094.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṅkato malyadharo suvattho, sukuṇḍalī kappitakesamassu;
```

```
Āmuttahatthābharaṇo yasassī, dibbe <pb ed="T" n="0.0123" /> vimānamhi yathāpi candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1095.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ, aṭṭhaṭṭhakā sikkhitā sādhurūpā;
```

```
Dibbā ca kaññā tidasacarā uḷārā, naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1096.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, disvāna samaṇe sīlavante;
```

```
Sampannavijjācaraṇe yasassī, bahussute taṇhakkhayūpapanne;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacitto, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1099.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="P" n="0.0108" /> metādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Paṭhamakuṇḍalīvimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

