#### 10. (Uttara) pāyāsivimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1108.</p>

```
‘‘Yā <pb ed="M" n="0.0102" /> devarājassa sabhā sudhammā, yatthacchati devasaṅgho samaggo;
```

```
Tathūpamaṃ tuyhamidaṃ vimānaṃ, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1109.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1110.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1111.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, rañño pāyāsissa ahosiṃ māṇavo;
```

```
Laddhā dhanaṃ saṃvibhāgaṃ akāsiṃ, piyā ca me sīlavanto ahesuṃ;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacitto, sakkacca <pb ed="T" n="0.0126" /> dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1112.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe. <pb ed="P" n="0.0110" /> …vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

(Uttara) pāyāsivimānaṃ <note>uttaravimānaṃ (sī. syā. aṭṭha.)</note> dasamaṃ.

Pāyāsivaggo chaṭṭho niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Dve agārino phaladāyī, dve upassayadāyī bhikkhāya dāyī;
```

```
Yavapālako ceva dve, kuṇḍalino pāyāsīti <note>pāṭhabhedo natthi</note>;
```

```
Purisānaṃ dutiyo vaggo pavuccatīti.
```

#### 7. Sunikkhittavaggo

#### 1. Cittalatāvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1114.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="M" n="0.0103" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0075" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0111" /> vanaṃ cittalataṃ pabhāsati, uyyānaseṭṭhaṃ tidasānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Tathūpamaṃ tuyhamidaṃ vimānaṃ, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1115.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1116.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… <pb ed="T" n="0.0127" /> yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1117.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, daliddo atāṇo kapaṇo kammakaro ahosiṃ;
```

```
Jiṇṇe ca mātāpitaro abhāriṃ <note>abhariṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, piyā ca me sīlavanto ahesuṃ;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacitto, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1118.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Cittalatāvimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Nandanavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1120.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="P" n="0.0112" /> vanaṃ nandanaṃ <note>nandanaṃ cittalataṃ (sī. syā. ka.), nandavanaṃ (ka.)</note> pabhāsati, uyyānaseṭṭhaṃ tidasānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Tathūpamaṃ tuyhamidaṃ vimānaṃ, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1121.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi <pb ed="M" n="0.0104" /> mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1122.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… <pb ed="T" n="0.0128" /> yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1123.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, daliddo atāṇo kapaṇo kammakaro ahosiṃ;
```

```
Jiṇṇe ca mātāpitaro abhāriṃ, piyā ca me sīlavanto ahesuṃ;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacitto, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1124.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="0.0076" /> metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Nandanavimānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Maṇithūṇavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1126.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0113" /> maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1127.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1128.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe…vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1130.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="0.0129" /> devaputto attamano…pe…yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1131.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0105" /> manussesu manussabhūto, vivane pathe saṅkamanaṃ <note>caṅkamanaṃ (sī.), caṅkamaṃ (syā.), samakaṃ (ka. sī.)</note> akāsiṃ;
```

```
Ārāmarukkhāni ca ropayissaṃ, piyā ca me sīlavanto ahesuṃ;
```

```
Annañca pānañca pasannacitto, sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1132.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Maṇithūṇavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Suvaṇṇavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1134.</p>

```
‘‘Sovaṇṇamaye <pb ed="P" n="0.0114" /> pabbatasmiṃ, vimānaṃ sabbatopabhaṃ;
```

```
Hemajālapaṭicchannaṃ <note>hemajālakapacchannaṃ (sī.)</note>, kiṅkiṇi <note>kiṅkaṇika (syā. ka.), kiṅkiṇika (pī.)</note> jālakappitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1135.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhaṃsā sukatā thambhā, sabbe veḷuriyāmayā;
```

```
Ekamekāya aṃsiyā, ratanā satta nimmitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1136.</p>

```
‘‘Veḷuriyasuvaṇṇassa, phalikā rūpiyassa ca;
```

```
Masāragallamuttāhi, lohitaṅgamaṇīhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1137.</p>

```
‘‘Citrā manoramā bhūmi, na tatthuddhaṃsatī rajo;
```

```
Gopāṇasīgaṇā pītā, kūṭaṃ dhārenti nimmitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1138.</p>

```
‘‘Sopāṇāni <pb ed="V" n="0.0077" /> ca cattāri, nimmitā caturo disā;
```

```
Nānāratanagabbhehi<pb ed="T" n="0.0130" />, ādiccova virocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1139.</p>

```
‘‘Vediyā catasso tattha, vibhattā bhāgaso mitā;
```

```
Daddallamānā ābhanti, samantā caturo disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1140.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmiṃ vimāne pavare, devaputto mahappabho;
```

```
Atirocasi vaṇṇena, udayantova bhāṇumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1141.</p>

```
‘‘Dānassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0106" /> te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
```

```
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1142.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1143.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ andhakavindasmiṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Vihāraṃ satthu kāresiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1144.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha gandhañca mālañca, paccayañca <note>paccaggañca (sī.), paccagghañca (?)</note> vilepanaṃ;
```

```
Vihāraṃ satthu adāsiṃ, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Tena mayhaṃ idaṃ laddhaṃ, vasaṃ vattemi nandane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1145.</p>

```
‘‘Nandane ca vane <note>nandane pavane (sī. syā.)</note> ramme, nānādijagaṇāyute;
```

```
Ramāmi naccagītehi, accharāhi purakkhato’’ti.
```

Suvaṇṇavimānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Ambavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1146.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0115" /> maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā <pb ed="T" n="0.0131" /> sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1147.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1148.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo…pe… vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1150.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1151.</p>

```
‘‘Gimhānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0107" /> pacchime māse, patapante <note>patāpante (syā.), patāpente (ka.)</note> divaṅkare;
```

```
Paresaṃ bhatako poso, ambārāmamasiñcati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1152.</p>

```
‘‘Atha <pb ed="V" n="0.0078" /> tenāgamā bhikkhu, sāriputtoti vissuto;
```

```
Kilantarūpo kāyena, akilantova cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1153.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca <pb ed="P" n="0.0116" /> disvāna āyantaṃ, avocaṃ ambasiñcako;
```

```
Sādhu taṃ <note>sādhukaṃ (ka.)</note> bhante nhāpeyyaṃ, yaṃ mamassa sukhāvahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1154.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa me anukampāya, nikkhipi pattacīvaraṃ;
```

```
Nisīdi rukkhamūlasmiṃ, chāyāya ekacīvaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1155.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca acchena vārinā, pasannamānaso naro;
```

```
Nhāpayī rukkhamūlasmiṃ, chāyāya ekacīvaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1156.</p>

```
‘‘Ambo <pb ed="T" n="0.0132" /> ca sitto samaṇo ca nhāpito, mayā ca puññaṃ pasutaṃ anappakaṃ;
```

```
Iti so pītiyā kāyaṃ, sabbaṃ pharati attano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1157.</p>

```
‘‘Tadeva ettakaṃ kammaṃ, akāsiṃ tāya jātiyā;
```

```
Pahāya mānusaṃ dehaṃ, upapannomhi nandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1158.</p>

```
‘‘Nandane ca vane ramme, nānādijagaṇāyute;
```

```
Ramāmi naccagītehi, accharāhi purakkhato’’ti.
```

Ambavimānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Gopālavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1159.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna devaṃ paṭipucchi bhikkhu, ucce vimānamhi ciraṭṭhitike;
```

```
Āmuttahatthābharaṇaṃ yasassiṃ <note>āmuttahatthābharaṇo yasassī (syā. pī. ka.)</note>, dibbe vimānamhi yathāpi candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1160.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṅkato <pb ed="M" n="0.0108" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0117" /> malyadharo <note>mālabhārī (sī.), māladharī (ka.)</note> suvattho, sukuṇḍalī kappitakesamassu;
```

```
Āmuttahatthābharaṇo yasassī, dibbe vimānamhi yathāpi candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1161.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ, aṭṭhaṭṭhakā sikkhitā sādhurūpā;
```

```
Dibbā ca kaññā tidasacarā uḷārā, naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1162.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1163.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="0.0133" /> devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1164.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto, saṅgamma rakkhissaṃ paresaṃ dhenuyo;
```

```
Tato ca āgā samaṇo mamantike gāvo ca māse agamaṃsu khādituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1165.</p>

```
‘‘Dvayajja <pb ed="V" n="0.0079" /> kiccaṃ ubhayañca kāriyaṃ, iccevahaṃ <note>iccevaṃ (ka.)</note> bhante tadā vicintayiṃ;
```

```
Tato ca saññaṃ paṭiladdhayoniso, dadāmi bhanteti khipiṃ anantakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1166.</p>

```
‘‘So māsakhettaṃ turito avāsariṃ, purā ayaṃ bhañjati yassidaṃ dhanaṃ;
```

```
Tato ca kaṇho urago mahāviso, aḍaṃsi pāde turitassa me sato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1167.</p>

```
‘‘Svāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0109" /> aṭṭomhi dukkhena pīḷito, bhikkhu ca taṃ sāmaṃ muñcitvānantakaṃ <note>muñcitva nantakaṃ (sī.), muñcitvā anantakaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Ahāsi kummāsaṃ mamānukampayā <note>mamānukampiyā (pī. ka.), mamānukampāya (syā.)</note>, tato cuto kālakatomhi devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1168.</p>

```
‘‘Tadeva <pb ed="T" n="0.0134" /> kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca kammaṃ anubhomi attanā;
```

```
Tayā hi bhante anukampito bhusaṃ, kataññutāya abhipādayāmi taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1169.</p>

```
‘‘Sadevake loke samārake ca, añño muni natthi tayānukampako;
```

```
Tayā hi bhante anukampito bhusaṃ, kataññutāya abhivādayāmi taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1170.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0118" /> loke parasmiṃ vā pana, añño munī natthi tayānukampako;
```

```
Tayā hi bhante anukampito bhusaṃ, kataññutāya abhivādayāmi ta’’nti.
```

Gopālavimānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Kaṇḍakavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1171.</p>

```
‘‘Puṇṇamāse yathā cando, nakkhattaparivārito;
```

```
Samantā anupariyāti, tārakādhipatī sasī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1172.</p>

```
‘‘Tathūpamaṃ idaṃ byamhaṃ, dibbaṃ devapuramhi ca;
```

```
Atirocati vaṇṇena, udayantova raṃsimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1173.</p>

```
‘‘Veḷuriyasuvaṇṇassa, phalikā rūpiyassa ca;
```

```
Masāragallamuttāhi, lohitaṅgamaṇīhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1174.</p>

```
‘‘Citrā manoramā bhūmi, veḷūriyassa santhatā;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā <pb ed="T" n="0.0135" /> subhā rammā, pāsādo te sumāpito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1175.</p>

```
‘‘Rammā <pb ed="M" n="0.0110" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0119" /> ca te pokkharaṇī, puthulomanisevitā;
```

```
Acchodakā vippasannā, sovaṇṇavālukasanthatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1176.</p>

```
‘‘Nānāpadumasañchannā, puṇḍarīkasamotatā <note>samotthatā (ka.), samogatā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Surabhiṃ sampavāyanti, manuññā māluteritā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1177.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā <pb ed="V" n="0.0080" /> te ubhato passe, vanagumbā sumāpitā;
```

```
Upetā puppharukkhehi, phalarukkhehi cūbhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1178.</p>

```
‘‘Sovaṇṇapāde pallaṅke, muduke goṇakatthate <note>colasanthate (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Nisinnaṃ devarājaṃva, upatiṭṭhanti accharā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1179.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbābharaṇasañchannā, nānāmālāvibhūsitā;
```

```
Ramenti taṃ mahiddhikaṃ, vasavattīva modasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1180.</p>

```
‘‘Bherisaṅkhamudiṅgāhi, vīṇāhi paṇavehi ca;
```

```
Ramasi ratisampanno, naccagīte suvādite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1181.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbā te vividhā rūpā, dibbā saddā atho rasā;
```

```
Gandhā ca te adhippetā, phoṭṭhabbā ca manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1182.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmiṃ vimāne pavare, devaputta mahappabho;
```

```
Atirocasi vaṇṇena, udayantova bhāṇumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1183.</p>

```
‘‘Dānassa te idaṃ phalaṃ, atho sīlassa vā pana;
```

```
Atho añjalikammassa, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1184.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="0.0136" /> devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1185.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ kapilavatthusmiṃ, sākiyānaṃ puruttame;
```

```
Suddhodanassa puttassa, kaṇḍako sahajo ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1186.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā so aḍḍharattāyaṃ, bodhāya mabhinikkhami;
```

```
So maṃ mudūhi pāṇīhi, jāli <note>jāla (sī.)</note> tambanakhehi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1187.</p>

```
‘‘Satthiṃ ākoṭayitvāna, vaha sammāti cabravi;
```

```
Ahaṃ lokaṃ tārayissaṃ, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1188.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0111" /> me giraṃ suṇantassa, hāso me vipulo ahu;
```

```
Udaggacitto sumano, abhisīsiṃ <note>abhisiṃsiṃ (sī.), abhisīsi (pī.)</note> tadā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1189.</p>

```
‘‘Abhirūḷhañca maṃ ñatvā, sakyaputtaṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Udaggacitto mudito, vahissaṃ purisuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1190.</p>

```
‘‘Paresaṃ vijitaṃ gantvā, uggatasmiṃ divākare <note>divaṅkare (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Mamaṃ channañca ohāya, anapekkho so apakkami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1191.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0120" /> tambanakhe pāde, jivhāya parilehisaṃ;
```

```
Gacchantañca mahāvīraṃ, rudamāno udikkhisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1192.</p>

```
‘‘Adassanenahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0081" /> tassa, sakyaputtassa sirīmato;
```

```
Alatthaṃ garukābādhaṃ, khippaṃ me maraṇaṃ ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1193.</p>

```
‘‘Tasseva ānubhāvena, vimānaṃ āvasāmidaṃ;
```

```
Sabbakāmaguṇopetaṃ<pb ed="T" n="0.0137" />, dibbaṃ devapuramhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1194.</p>

```
‘‘Yañca me ahuvā hāso, saddaṃ sutvāna bodhiyā;
```

```
Teneva kusalamūlena, phusissaṃ āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1195.</p>

```
‘‘Sace hi bhante gaccheyyāsi, satthu buddhassa santike;
```

```
Mamāpi naṃ vacanena, sirasā vajjāsi vandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1196.</p>

```
‘‘Ahampi daṭṭhuṃ gacchissaṃ, jinaṃ appaṭipuggalaṃ;
```

```
Dullabhaṃ dassanaṃ hoti, lokanāthāna tādina’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1197.</p>

```
So kataññū katavedī, satthāraṃ upasaṅkami;
```

```
Sutvā giraṃ cakkhumato, dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1198.</p>

```
Visodhetvā diṭṭhigataṃ, vicikicchaṃ vatāni ca;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, tatthevantaradhāyathāti <note>tatthevantaradhāyatīti (ka.)</note>.
```

Kaṇḍakavimānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Anekavaṇṇavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1199.</p>

```
‘‘Anekavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0112" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0121" /> darasokanāsanaṃ, vimānamāruyha anekacittaṃ;
```

```
Parivārito accharāsaṅgaṇena, sunimmito bhūtapatīva modasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1200.</p>

```
‘‘Samassamo natthi kuto panuttaro <note>uttari (ka.)</note>, yasena puññena ca iddhiyā ca;
```

```
Sabbe ca devā tidasagaṇā samecca, taṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0138" /> taṃ namassanti sasiṃva devā;
```

```
Imā ca te accharāyo samantato, naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1201.</p>

```
‘‘Deviddhipattosi <pb ed="P" n="0.0122" /> mahānubhāvo, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1202.</p>

```
So devaputto attamano…pe… yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1203.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ bhadante ahuvāsi pubbe, sumedhanāmassa jinassa sāvako;
```

```
Puthujjano ananubodhohamasmi <note>anavabodhohamasmiṃ (sī.), ananubodhohamāsiṃ (?)</note>, so satta vassāni paribbajissahaṃ <note>pabbajissahaṃ (syā. ka.), pabbajisāhaṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1204.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0082" /> sumedhassa jinassa satthuno, parinibbutassoghatiṇṇassa tādino;
```

```
Ratanuccayaṃ hemajālena channaṃ, vanditvā thūpasmiṃ manaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1205.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="0.0113" /> māsi dānaṃ na ca matthi dātuṃ, pare ca kho tattha samādapesiṃ;
```

```
Pūjetha naṃ pūjanīyassa <note>pūjaneyyassa (syā. ka.)</note> dhātuṃ, evaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0139" /> kira saggamito gamissatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1206.</p>

```
‘‘Tadeva kammaṃ kusalaṃ kataṃ mayā, sukhañca dibbaṃ anubhomi attanā;
```

```
Modāmahaṃ tidasagaṇassa majjhe, na tassa puññassa khayampi ajjhaga’’nti.
```

Anekavaṇṇavimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Maṭṭhakuṇḍalīvimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1207.</p>

```
<note>pe. va. 186</note> ‘‘Alaṅkato <pb ed="P" n="0.0123" /> maṭṭhakuṇḍalī <note>maṭṭakuṇḍalī (sī.)</note>, māladhārī haricandanussado;
```

```
Bāhā paggayha kandasi, vanamajjhe kiṃ dukkhito tuva’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1208.</p>

```
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayo pabhassaro, uppanno rathapañjaro mama;
```

```
Tassa cakkayugaṃ na vindāmi, tena dukkhena jahāmi <note>jahissaṃ (sī.), jahissāmi (syā. pī.)</note> jīvita’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1209.</p>

```
‘‘Sovaṇṇamayaṃ maṇimayaṃ, lohitakamayaṃ <note>lohitaṅgamayaṃ (syā.), lohitaṅkamayaṃ (sī.), lohamayaṃ (katthaci)</note> atha rūpiyamayaṃ;
```

```
Ācikkha <note>ācikkhatha (ka.)</note> me bhaddamāṇava, cakkayugaṃ paṭipādayāmi te’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1210.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="0.0140" /> māṇavo tassa pāvadi, ‘‘candimasūriyā ubhayettha dissare;
```

```
Sovaṇṇamayo ratho mama, tena cakkayugena sobhatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1211.</p>

```
‘‘Bālo <pb ed="M" n="0.0114" /> kho tvaṃ asi māṇava, yo tvaṃ patthayase apatthiyaṃ;
```

```
Maññāmi tuvaṃ marissasi, na hi tvaṃ lacchasi candimasūriye’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1212.</p>

```
‘‘Gamanāgamanampi dissati, vaṇṇadhātu ubhayattha vīthiyā;
```

```
Peto <note>peto pana (sī. syā.)</note> kālakato na dissati, ko nidha kandataṃ bālyataro’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1213.</p>

```
‘‘Saccaṃ kho vadesi māṇava, ahameva kandataṃ bālyataro;
```

```
Candaṃ viya dārako rudaṃ, petaṃ kālakatābhipatthayi’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1214.</p>

```
‘‘Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
```

```
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1215.</p>

```
‘‘Abbahī <pb ed="T" n="0.0141" /> <note>abbūḷha (pī.), abbūḷhaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> vata me sallaṃ, sokaṃ hadayanissitaṃ;
```

```
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1216.</p>

```
‘‘Svāhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0083" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0124" /> abbūḷhasallosmi, sītibhūtosmi nibbuto;
```

```
Na socāmi na rodāmi, vata sutvāna māṇavāti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1217.</p>

```
‘‘Devatā nusi gandhabbo, adu <note>ādu (sī. syā.)</note> sakko purindado;
```

```
Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1218.</p>

```
‘‘Yañca <note>yaṃ (ka.)</note> kandasi yañca rodasi, puttaṃ āḷāhane sayaṃ dahitvā;
```

```
Svāhaṃ kusalaṃ karitvā kammaṃ, tidasānaṃ sahabyataṃ gato’’ti <note>pattoti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1219.</p>

```
‘‘Appaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0115" /> vā bahuṃ vā nāddasāma, dānaṃ dadantassa sake agāre;
```

```
Uposathakammaṃ vā <note>uposathakammañca (ka.)</note> tādisaṃ, kena kammena gatosi devaloka’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1220.</p>

```
‘‘Ābādhikohaṃ dukkhito gilāno, āturarūpomhi sake nivesane;
```

```
Buddhaṃ vigatarajaṃ vitiṇṇakaṅkhaṃ, addakkhiṃ sugataṃ anomapaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1221 .</p>

```
‘‘Svāhaṃ muditamano pasannacitto, añjaliṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0142" /> akariṃ tathāgatassa;
```

```
Tāhaṃ kusalaṃ karitvāna kammaṃ, tidasānaṃ sahabyataṃ gato’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1222.</p>

```
‘‘Acchariyaṃ vata abbhutaṃ vata, añjalikammassa ayamīdiso vipāko;
```

```
Ahampi muditamano pasannacitto, ajjeva buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ vajāmī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1223.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjeva buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ vajāhi, dhammañca saṅghañca pasannacitto;
```

```
Tatheva sikkhāya padāni pañca, akhaṇḍaphullāni samādiyassu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1224.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā viramassu khippaṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayassu;
```

```
Amajjapo mā ca musā bhaṇāhi, sakena dārena ca hohi tuṭṭho’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1225.</p>

```
‘‘Atthakāmosi me yakkha, hitakāmosi devate;
```

```
Karomi tuyhaṃ vacanaṃ, tvaṃsi ācariyo mamāti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1226.</p>

```
‘‘Upemi saraṇaṃ buddhaṃ, dhammañcāpi anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Saṅghañca naradevassa, gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1227.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇātipātā <pb ed="M" n="0.0116" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0125" /> viramāmi khippaṃ, loke <pb ed="T" n="0.0143" /> adinnaṃ parivajjayāmi;
```

```
Amajjapo no ca musā bhaṇāmi, sakena dārena ca homi tuṭṭho’’ti.
```

Maṭṭhakuṇḍalīvimānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Serīsakavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1228.</p>

```
<note>pe. va. 604</note> Suṇotha <pb ed="V" n="0.0084" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0126" /> yakkhassa ca vāṇijāna ca, samāgamo yattha tadā ahosi;
```

```
Yathā kathaṃ itaritarena cāpi, subhāsitaṃ tañca suṇātha sabbe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1229.</p>

```
‘‘Yo so ahu rājā pāyāsi nāma <note>nāmo (sī.)</note>, bhummānaṃ sahabyagato yasassī;
```

```
So modamānova sake vimāne, amānuso mānuse ajjhabhāsīti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1230.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṅke araññe amanussaṭṭhāne, kantāre appodake appabhakkhe;
```

```
Suduggame vaṇṇupathassa majjhe, vaṅkaṃ bhayā <note>dhaṅkaṃbhayā (ka.)</note> naṭṭhamanā manussā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1231.</p>

```
‘‘Nayidha phalā mūlamayā ca santi, upādānaṃ natthi kutodha bhakkho;
```

```
Aññatra paṃsūhi ca vālukāhi ca, tatāhi <pb ed="T" n="0.0144" /> uṇhāhi ca dāruṇāhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1232.</p>

```
‘‘Ujjaṅgalaṃ tattamivaṃ kapālaṃ, anāyasaṃ paralokena tulyaṃ;
```

```
Luddānamāvāsamidaṃ purāṇaṃ, bhūmippadeso abhisattarūpo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1233.</p>

```
‘‘Atha <pb ed="M" n="0.0117" /> tumhe kena <note>kena nu (syā. ka.)</note> vaṇṇena, kimāsamānā imaṃ padesaṃ hi;
```

```
Anupaviṭṭhā sahasā samecca, lobhā bhayā atha vā sampamūḷhā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1234.</p>

```
‘‘Magadhesu aṅgesu ca satthavāhā, āropayitvā paṇiyaṃ puthuttaṃ;
```

```
Te yāmase sindhusovīrabhūmiṃ, dhanatthikā uddayaṃ patthayānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1235.</p>

```
‘‘Divā <pb ed="P" n="0.0127" /> pipāsaṃ nadhivāsayantā, yoggānukampañca samekkhamānā,
```

```
Etena vegena āyāma sabbe <note>sabbe te (ka.)</note>, rattiṃ maggaṃ paṭipannā vikāle.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1236.</p>

```
‘‘Te duppayātā aparaddhamaggā, andhākulā vippanaṭṭhā araññe;
```

```
Suduggame <pb ed="T" n="0.0145" /> vaṇṇupathassa majjhe, disaṃ na jānāma pamūḷhacittā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1237.</p>

```
‘‘Idañca disvāna adiṭṭhapubbaṃ, vimānaseṭṭhañca tavañca yakkha;
```

```
Tatuttariṃ jīvitamāsamānā, disvā patītā sumanā udaggā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1238.</p>

```
‘‘Pāraṃ samuddassa imañca vaṇṇuṃ <note>vanaṃ (syā.), vaṇṇaṃ (ka.)</note>, vettācaraṃ <note>vettaṃ paraṃ (syā.), vettācāraṃ (ka.)</note> saṅkupathañca maggaṃ;
```

```
Nadiyo pana pabbatānañca duggā, puthuddisā gacchatha bhogahetu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1239.</p>

```
‘‘Pakkhandiyāna vijitaṃ paresaṃ, verajjake mānuse pekkhamānā;
```

```
Yaṃ vo sutaṃ vā atha vāpi diṭṭhaṃ, accherakaṃ taṃ vo suṇoma tātā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1240.</p>

```
‘‘Itopi <pb ed="M" n="0.0118" /> accherataraṃ kumāra, na to sutaṃ vā atha vāpi diṭṭhaṃ;
```

```
Atītamānussakameva sabbaṃ, disvāna tappāma anomavaṇṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1241.</p>

```
‘‘Vehāyasaṃ pokkharañño savanti, pahūtamalyā <pb ed="T" n="0.0146" /> <note>pahūtamālyā (syā.)</note> bahupuṇḍarīkā;
```

```
Dumā cime <note>dumā ca te (syā. ka.)</note> niccaphalūpapannā, atīva gandhā surabhiṃ pavāyanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1242.</p>

```
‘‘Veḷūriyathambhā <pb ed="V" n="0.0085" /> satamussitāse, silāpavāḷassa ca āyataṃsā;
```

```
Masāragallā sahalohitaṅgā, thambhā ime jotirasāmayāse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1243.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassathambhaṃ atulānubhāvaṃ, tesūpari sādhumidaṃ vimānaṃ;
```

```
Ratanantaraṃ kañcanavedimissaṃ, tapanīyapaṭṭehi ca sādhuchannaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1244.</p>

```
‘‘Jambonaduttattamidaṃ sumaṭṭho, pāsādasopāṇaphalūpapanno;
```

```
Daḷho ca vaggu ca susaṅgato ca <note>vaggu sumukho susaṅgato (sī.)</note>, atīva nijjhānakhamo manuñño.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1245.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanantarasmiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0128" /> bahuannapānaṃ, parivārito accharāsaṅgaṇena;
```

```
Murajaālambaratūriyaghuṭṭho, abhivanditosi thutivandanāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1246.</p>

```
‘‘So <pb ed="T" n="0.0147" /> modasi nārigaṇappabodhano, vimānapāsādavare manorame;
```

```
Acintiyo sabbaguṇūpapanno, rājā yathā vessavaṇo naḷinyā <note>naḷiññaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1247.</p>

```
‘‘Devo <pb ed="M" n="0.0119" /> nu āsi udavāsi yakkho, udāhu devindo manussabhūto;
```

```
Pucchanti taṃ vāṇijā satthavāhā, ācikkha ko nāma tuvaṃsi yakkho’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1248.</p>

```
‘‘Serīsako <note>serissako (sī. syā.)</note> nāma ahamhi yakkho, kantāriyo vaṇṇupathamhi gutto;
```

```
Imaṃ padesaṃ abhipālayāmi, vacanakaro vessavaṇassa rañño’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1249.</p>

```
‘‘Adhiccaladdhaṃ pariṇāmajaṃ te, sayaṃ kataṃ udāhu devehi dinnaṃ;
```

```
Pucchanti taṃ vāṇijā satthavāhā, kathaṃ tayā laddhamidaṃ manuñña’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1250.</p>

```
‘‘Nādhiccaladdhaṃ na pariṇāmajaṃ me, na sayaṃ kataṃ na hi devehi dinnaṃ;
```

```
Sakehi kammehi apāpakehi, puññehi <pb ed="T" n="0.0148" /> me laddhamidaṃ manuñña’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1251.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
```

```
Pucchanti taṃ vāṇijā satthavāhā, kathaṃ tayā laddhamidaṃ vimāna’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1252.</p>

```
‘‘Mamaṃ pāyāsīti ahu samaññā, rajjaṃ yadā kārayiṃ kosalānaṃ;
```

```
Natthikadiṭṭhi kadariyo pāpadhammo, ucchedavādī ca tadā ahosiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1253.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇo ca kho āsi kumārakassapo, bahussuto cittakathī uḷāro;
```

```
So me tadā dhammakathaṃ abhāsi <note>akāsi (sī.)</note>, diṭṭhivisūkāni vinodayī me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1254.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0120" /> tassa <note>tāhaṃ (ka.)</note> dhammakathaṃ suṇitvā, upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayissaṃ;
```

```
Pāṇātipātā virato ahosiṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayissaṃ;
```

```
Amajjapo <pb ed="P" n="0.0129" /> no ca musā abhāṇiṃ, sakena dārena ca ahosi tuṭṭho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1255.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0149" /> me vataṃ taṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, tassa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
```

```
Teheva kammehi apāpakehi, puññehi me laddhamidaṃ vimāna’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1256.</p>

```
‘‘Saccaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0086" /> kirāhaṃsu narā sapaññā, anaññathā vacanaṃ paṇḍitānaṃ;
```

```
Yahiṃ yahiṃ gacchati puññakammo, tahiṃ tahiṃ modati kāmakāmī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1257.</p>

```
‘‘Yahiṃ yahiṃ sokapariddavo ca, vadho ca bandho ca parikkileso;
```

```
Tahiṃ tahiṃ gacchati pāpakammo, na muccati duggatiyā kadācī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1258.</p>

```
‘‘Sammūḷharūpova jano ahosi, asmiṃ muhutte kalalīkatova;
```

```
Janassimassa tuyhañca kumāra, appaccayo kena nu kho ahosī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1259.</p>

```
‘‘Ime ca sirīsavanā <note>ime sirīsūpavanā ca (sī.), imepi sirīsavanā ca (pī. ka.)</note> tātā, dibbā <note>dibbā ca (pī. ka.)</note> gandhā surabhī <note>surabhiṃ (sī. ka.)</note> sampavanti <note>sampavāyanti (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Te sampavāyanti imaṃ vimānaṃ, divā <pb ed="T" n="0.0150" /> ca ratto ca tamaṃ nihantvā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1260.</p>

```
‘‘Imesañca <pb ed="M" n="0.0121" /> kho vassasataccayena, sipāṭikā phalati ekamekā;
```

```
Mānussakaṃ vassasataṃ atītaṃ, yadagge kāyamhi idhūpapanno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1261.</p>

```
‘‘Disvānahaṃ vassasatāni pañca, asmiṃ vimāne ṭhatvāna tātā;
```

```
Āyukkhayā puññakkhayā cavissaṃ, teneva sokena pamucchitosmī’’ti <note>samucchitosmīti (pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1262.</p>

```
‘‘Kathaṃ nu soceyya tathāvidho so, laddhā vimānaṃ atulaṃ cirāya;
```

```
Ye cāpi kho ittaramupapannā, te nūna soceyyuṃ parittapuññā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1263.</p>

```
‘‘Anucchaviṃ ovadiyañca me taṃ, yaṃ maṃ tumhe peyyavācaṃ vadetha;
```

```
Tumhe ca kho tātā mayānuguttā, yenicchakaṃ tena paletha sotthi’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1264.</p>

```
‘‘Gantvā <pb ed="P" n="0.0130" /> mayaṃ sindhusovīrabhūmiṃ, dhanatthikā uddayaṃ patthayānā;
```

```
Yathāpayogā paripuṇṇacāgā, kāhāma <pb ed="T" n="0.0151" /> serīsamahaṃ uḷāra’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1265.</p>

```
‘‘Mā ceva serīsamahaṃ akattha, sabbañca vo bhavissati yaṃ vadetha;
```

```
Pāpāni kammāni vivajjayātha, dhammānuyogañca adhiṭṭhahātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1266.</p>

```
‘‘Upāsako atthi imamhi saṅghe, bahussuto sīlavatūpapanno;
```

```
Saddho ca cāgī ca supesalo ca, vicakkhaṇo santusito mutīmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1267.</p>

```
‘‘Sañjānamāno <pb ed="M" n="0.0122" /> na musā bhaṇeyya, parūpaghātāya na cetayeyya;
```

```
Vebhūtikaṃ pesuṇaṃ no kareyya, saṇhañca vācaṃ sakhilaṃ bhaṇeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1268.</p>

```
‘‘Sagāravo sappaṭisso vinīto, apāpako adhisīle visuddho;
```

```
So mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi jantu, dhammena poseti ariyavutti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1269.</p>

```
‘‘Maññe so mātāpitūnaṃ kāraṇā, bhogāni pariyesati na attahetu;
```

```
Mātāpitūnañca yo <note>so (?)</note> accayena, nekkhammapoṇo <pb ed="T" n="0.0152" /> carissati brahmacariyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1270.</p>

```
‘‘Ujū avaṅko asaṭho amāyo, na lesakappena ca vohareyya;
```

```
So tādiso sukatakammakārī, dhamme ṭhito kinti labhetha dukkhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1271.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0087" /> kāraṇā pātukatomhi attanā, tasmā dhammaṃ passatha vāṇijāse;
```

```
Aññatra teniha bhasmī <note>bhasmi (syā.), bhasma (ka.)</note> bhavetha, andhākulā vippanaṭṭhā araññe;
```

```
Taṃ khippamānena lahuṃ parena, sukho have sappurisena saṅgamo’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1272.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ nāma so kiñca karoti kammaṃ,
```

```
Kiṃ nāmadheyyaṃ kiṃ pana tassa gottaṃ;
```

```
Mayampi naṃ daṭṭhukāmamha yakkha, yassānukampāya idhāgatosi;
```

```
Lābhā hi tassa, yassa tuvaṃ pihesī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1273.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="M" n="0.0123" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0131" /> kappako sambhavanāmadheyyo,
```

```
Upāsako kocchaphalūpajīvī;
```

```
Jānātha naṃ tumhākaṃ pesiyo so,
```

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="0.0153" /> kho naṃ hīḷittha supesalo so’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1274.</p>

```
‘‘Jānāmase yaṃ tvaṃ pavadesi <note>vadesi (sī.)</note> yakkha,
```

```
Na kho naṃ jānāma sa edisoti;
```

```
Mayampi naṃ pūjayissāma yakkha,
```

```
Sutvāna tuyhaṃ vacanaṃ uḷāra’’nti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1275.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci imasmiṃ satthe manussā,
```

```
Daharā mahantā athavāpi majjhimā;
```

```
Sabbeva te ālambantu vimānaṃ,
```

```
Passantu puññānaṃ phalaṃ kadariyā’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1276.</p>

```
Te tattha sabbeva ‘ahaṃ pure’ti,
```

```
Taṃ kappakaṃ tattha purakkhatvā <note>purakkhipitvā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbeva te ālambiṃsu vimānaṃ,
```

```
Masakkasāraṃ viya vāsavassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1277.</p>

```
Te <pb ed="T" n="0.0154" /> tattha sabbeva ‘ahaṃ pure’ti, upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayiṃsu;
```

```
Pāṇātipātā viratā ahesuṃ, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayiṃsu;
```

```
Amajjapā no ca musā bhaṇiṃsu, sakena dārena ca ahesuṃ tuṭṭhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1278.</p>

```
Te tattha sabbeva ‘ahaṃ pure’ti, upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayitvā;
```

```
Pakkāmi sattho anumodamāno, yakkhiddhiyā anumato punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1279.</p>

```
‘‘Gantvāna <pb ed="M" n="0.0124" /> te sindhusovīrabhūmiṃ, dhanatthikā uddayaṃ <note>udaya (pī. ka.)</note> patthayānā;
```

```
Yathāpayogā paripuṇṇalābhā, paccāgamuṃ pāṭaliputtamakkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1280.</p>

```
‘‘Gantvāna <pb ed="V" n="0.0088" /> te saṅgharaṃ sotthivanto,
```

```
Puttehi dārehi samaṅgibhūtā;
```

```
Ānandī vittā <note>ānandacittā (syā.), ānandīcittā (ka.)</note> sumanā patītā,
```

```
Akaṃsu serīsamahaṃ uḷāraṃ;
```

```
Serīsakaṃ te pariveṇaṃ māpayiṃsu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1281.</p>

```
Etādisā sappurisāna sevanā,
```

```
Mahatthikā dhammaguṇāna sevanā;
```

```
Ekassa atthāya upāsakassa,
```

```
Sabbeva sattā sukhitā <note>sukhino (pī. ka.)</note> ahesunti.
```

Serīsakavimānaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 11. Sunikkhittavimānavatthu

<p rend="hangnum">§1282.</p>

```
‘‘Uccamidaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0134" /> maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ, samantato dvādasa yojanāni;
```

```
Kūṭāgārā <pb ed="T" n="0.0155" /> sattasatā uḷārā, veḷuriyathambhā rucakatthatā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1283.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthacchasi pivasi khādasi ca, dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vagguṃ;
```

```
Dibbā rasā kāmaguṇettha pañca, nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1284.</p>

```
‘‘Kena tetādiso vaṇṇo, kena te idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te bhogā, ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1285.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0125" /> ‘taṃ deva mahānubhāva, manussabhūto kimakāsi puññaṃ;
```

```
Kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo, vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1286.</p>

```
So <pb ed="P" n="0.0135" /> devaputto attamano, moggallānena pucchito;
```

```
Pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi, yassa kammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1287.</p>

```
‘‘Dunnikkhittaṃ mālaṃ sunikkhipitvā, patiṭṭhapetvā sugatassa thūpe;
```

```
Mahiddhiko camhi mahānubhāvo, dibbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1288.</p>

```
‘‘Tena metādiso vaṇṇo,
```

```
Tena me idha mijjhati;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca me bhogā,
```

```
Ye keci manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1289.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva,
```

```
Manussabhūto yamahaṃ akāsiṃ;
```

```
Tenamhi <pb ed="T" n="0.0156" /> evaṃ jalitānubhāvo,
```

```
Vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī’’ti.
```

Sunikkhittavimānaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

Sunikkhittavaggo sattamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0089" /> –

```
Dve daliddā vanavihārā, bhatako gopālakaṇḍakā;
```

```
Anekavaṇṇamaṭṭhakuṇḍalī, serīsako sunikkhittaṃ;
```

```
Purisānaṃ tatiyo vaggo pavuccatīti.
```

Bhāṇavāraṃ catutthaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Vimānavatthupāḷi niṭṭhitā.</trailer>
